ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1225&endYear=1225')">1225年</a>　在广州。再荐于乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3a788ae68bc24a848a603453f2250353_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3a788ae68bc24a848a603453f2250353");'><span id='3a788ae68bc24a848a603453f2250353_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: /></div><div class='label1' id='e74ccce70c0f4692ad2622d1d3cd7f95_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e74ccce70c0f4692ad2622d1d3cd7f95");'><span id='e74ccce70c0f4692ad2622d1d3cd7f95_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1236')">1232-1236年</a>，32-36岁</div><div id='e74ccce70c0f4692ad2622d1d3cd7f95' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年10月23日</a>　在广州。继母潘氏卒，丁母艰，归广州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年</a>　在广州。四子性道生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1233&endYear=1233')">1233年</a>　在广州。丁继母艰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1234&endYear=1234')">1234年5月1日</a>　在广州。有文一篇。作品：义鹿记。<div id='poem_1312904' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312904' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312904?labeling=true' target='_blank'>义鹿记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1234年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312904")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312904_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312904'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312904'>端平之元夏五朔，府帅曾公纵鹿二于白云山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312904_comment'></div>昨岁六月十日，菊坡先生寿公物也，始豢之郡圃，攸伏，既入层林荟翳间，噳噳得所，犹屡顾不忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312904_comment'></div>逾月，邦人争炉瓣芗祝初度，颂声欢雷，和气熏春，方称觥公堂，鹿雄雌追随，繇城北隅复遄绕旂幢，呦鸣伎跃如舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312904_comment'></div>已去四十日，诘屈二十里，是胡为来，若五仙羊导之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312904_comment'></div>万众诧诩，属某笔一段奇事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312904_comment'></div>夫物各性其天，惟至诚能尽物之性，乐忭百兽，信孚豚鱼，不期然而然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312904_comment'></div>公莅广，其政仁，视民物不二，推俸倾橐，廪饥赈穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312904_comment'></div>充是心，将使飞潜动植咸若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312904_comment'></div>鹿尝侣西归，龟鹤来处已不凡，矧圃贤牧德宇中，宜若是谊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312904_comment'></div>古循吏白鹿随车，岂诞且诬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312904_comment'></div>物恋恋不忘，人心爱怀，又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312904_comment'></div>然公非姑息为仁，狌鼯啸林，鲸鲵舞海，稍出奇略，一网成禽，锄奸束猾，弗宥毫缕，固异夫内欺校人，惠而不知为政者云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312904_comment'></div>公名治凤，字君辉，清源人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312904_comment'></div>番禺李昴英记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1312904_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1234&endYear=1234')">1234年</a>　在广州，丁继母艰。五子由道生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1233&endYear=1233')">1233年</a>　在广州。李春叟从其学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　在广州。服除，除武学博士，未赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年2月</a>　在广州。摧锋军围广州，缒城谕贼，贼退。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1235&endYear=1235')">1235年</a>　在广州。平叛事闻于朝，除大理司直。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年1月1日</a>　在临安。有文一篇。作品：诗隐楼记。<div id='poem_1312905' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312905' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312905?labeling=true' target='_blank'>诗隐楼记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1236年1月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312905")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312905_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312905'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312905'>何谓隐？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312905_comment'></div>自适其安而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312905_comment'></div>庐人境而襟物表，奚必蹈高遁远哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312905_comment'></div>吾友昭武黄君希声工晚唐诗，游五羊，获登菊坡先生门，因筑舍其旁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312905_comment'></div>前为重楼，俯坡山，控越冈，萃堵坡童童如䨥笔书空，树林远近，罨画成图，碧瓦差池，玻璃千顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312905_comment'></div>地据三城正中，四面平远，故宜楼，揭李、杜写真，贮唐人诗卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312905_comment'></div>至人寄目天末，拥鼻风前，一景物之歆，一兴趣之味，尽入句眼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312905_comment'></div>方其会心得意，且不知身之楼居，而何有耳之市声耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312905_comment'></div>字楼以诗隐，其志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312905_comment'></div>或谓昔人之市其隐者，君平以卜，伯休以药，诗则未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312905_comment'></div>盖红尘浩荡中，未免催租人至，非灞桥雪中驴上，何处有诗？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312905_comment'></div>余则曰心有动静，地无喧寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312905_comment'></div>阮籍竹林之游，王戎后至，籍曰「俗子来，殊败人意」，戎谓如卿之意，政易败耳，此山林而动者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312905_comment'></div>贾浪仙鍊敲推二字，触京尹前导而不知，此城府而静者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312905_comment'></div>诗隐主人，其浪仙后身乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312905_comment'></div>矧才高志大，不止嚬呻痛痒，属者顽童叫突，菊坡起帅乡部，绣使彭公督师，衔密画往来其间，迄清乱略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312905_comment'></div>闲则诗人，用则国士，潜虽伏矣，亦孔之昭，希声自此不得隐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312905_comment'></div>希声名镛，其诗有《樵溪初藁》云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312905_comment'></div>端平丙申元日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1312905_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年1月15日</a>　在临安，有词。作品：沁园春（才到中年）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3bd08721d3e145088385ad8c4b9c9e9c_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3bd08721d3e145088385ad8c4b9c9e9c");'><span id='3bd08721d3e145088385ad8c4b9c9e9c_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1244')">1243-1244年</a>，43-44岁</div><div id='3bd08721d3e145088385ad8c4b9c9e9c' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：题节推张端义荃翁集。跋吴都统所藏菊坡先生帖。题郑南瑞砾铁集。<div id='poem_1312887' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312887' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312887?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题节推张端义荃翁集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312887")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312887_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312887'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312887'>士行乎患难，可以验学力所至深浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312887_comment'></div>苟闻道矣，虽濒于死不变，有饱鸡粥，鼾睡以须者，羁困旅逆，又焉能动其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312887_comment'></div>姑苏张君端义，以选人三上书帝阍，最后书言最狂，端平明禋雷雨时也，天子戆之，仅于韶以置，乃得与监门侠谪所邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312887_comment'></div>老矣落南，依败屋，然破釜竹榻纸衿，凄其谁堪，而颜丹如，气虹如，不作憔悴无聊状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312887_comment'></div>其诗累篇骨处实，眼处活，峭奇而非怪，含婉而不怒，多从胸中书流出，他日将与名相久远，而后知数年数千里外，所以充充然自适，而忘秋风莼鲈之感者，心寄于诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312887_comment'></div>或问《离骚》荃喻其王，而君荃翁号何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312887_comment'></div>余应之曰：「荃，香草也，特寓焉以自别于薋葹辈耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312887_comment'></div>周大君在上，楚莫非臣，是于义无嫌」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312887_comment'></div>淳祐三年重九，文溪李昴英书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312887_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312876' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312876' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312876?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋吴都统所藏菊坡先生帖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312876")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312876_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312876'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312876'>清献崔公护坤维，晚必自出伺烽火，至报稍急，辄通夕不寐，思所以应，乃心无顷刻忘边忧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312876_comment'></div>指纵诸将，每手笔驿以授，情通如家人，而人乐为之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312876_comment'></div>都统吴侯彦公所识，擢荐之之词曰「宣力边防，轻财得士卒心」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312876_comment'></div>介胄之士才且廉，世不多得，公以清勤身帅之验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312876_comment'></div>是时全蜀如金瓯，无少玷缺，续貂以狗，而贻祸遂至于不可救药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312876_comment'></div>吴侯久已摈去，流落天南，邂逅共谈西事，慷慨愤激，有老马千里志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312876_comment'></div>归斯人于乡国，使经理残碎地，岂不愈于用新进辈哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312876_comment'></div>同时有李侯绅，受知于公，后以死节闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312876_comment'></div>公知人之明类此，故并识之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312876_comment'></div>淳祐三年良月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312876_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312888' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312888' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312888?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郑南瑞砾铁集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1243年11月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312888")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312888_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312888'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312888'>铁随取而有，人得而凡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312888_comment'></div>然极其至精，有天下至宝不能当者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312888_comment'></div>一剑而敌，千金已珍矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312888_comment'></div>一鼎而寿，国且千祀，谁得而价哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312888_comment'></div>闻郑君南瑞标所业曰「砾铁」，自谓其文如铁藏沙砾中，俟淘鍊之工而未遇也，意则甚谦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312888_comment'></div>铁亦岂易方耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312888_comment'></div>能坚其志，刚其气，学成而器于时，则肠焉宋广平，面焉赵清献，可不朽百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312888_comment'></div>彼锥以刺，砚以磨，徒欲资笔舌铮铮旦暮间，君子不贵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312888_comment'></div>返其行卷，书以厉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312888_comment'></div>若曰铸人，则予不敢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312888_comment'></div>淳祐三年十一月十三日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1312888_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1243&endYear=1243')">1243年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：送荃翁张端义之惠阳。即席和人送荃翁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年1月15日</a>　在广州。有词。作品：瑞鹤仙（玉城春不夜）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年2月1日</a>　在广州。有文。作品：东莞县学经史阁记。<div id='poem_1312898' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312898' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312898?labeling=true' target='_blank'>东莞县学经史阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312898")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312898_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312898'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312898'>莞号广闻邑，罗浮址之，厚海负之，钜产秀民为多，设学宜称是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312898_comment'></div>淳熙此焉始基，开禧丙寅迁大成殿于西，嘉定辛巳因移黉舍其前，面势视厥初差易位而当胜处，至绍定己丑而后对辟斋庐，重作南门，才具体而微，亦艰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312898_comment'></div>世俗吏类急期会，迂化本，鞠蔬积弗治，老屋将压，新筑亦敝，何易也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312898_comment'></div>温陵许公以海内大儒来为宰，士相庆曰：「吾邑其幸乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312898_comment'></div>吾道其泰乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312898_comment'></div>嘉熙之元元日，公始庙谒，喟庠序圮陋，谓第一义不可皋，出来橐十万，授监河张君朴庀缮其事，繇殿而庑，而祭器库，而门，而庖，而湢，鼎鼎伟观，乃躬程试，收其隽尤，育之淑之，员倍给腆，衿佩自远方至者于于，弦歌洋洋，前此未有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312898_comment'></div>邑有没入之田一顷八十三亩有奇，金银为钱五十万有奇，法当上之宪台，公请并归于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312898_comment'></div>绣衣吴公旂素敬公，慨然弗靳，继粟益裕，以其钱即直庐而阁其上，轮奂雄峙，博收图籍庋之，万签森架，士得读所未见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312898_comment'></div>餫使陈公畴亦捐三十万相厥役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312898_comment'></div>又不足，则鸠节用之赢资其成，成而虞其坏，储十万为后日补饬费，虑周矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312898_comment'></div>学垂百年，草创未完，公一手营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312898_comment'></div>学田阅几令漠不问，公独能增益之，然皆其馀事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312898_comment'></div>公之学，得伊洛、紫阳之心传，所至山斗后进，异时横经番山，规矩严，条教悉，日夜至斋房与诸生讲论，有一艺能，极口称奖，不中不才者，亦循循善诱，卒使为成人，一时席间士，皆卓然有立，广人德之深，共建生祠于泮宫之东，至今朔望罗拜其下如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312898_comment'></div>菊坡清献公自蜀归，闻而嘉叹，方言状于朝，时未识公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312898_comment'></div>公兹来，莞人孚其德望，民曰「吾父也」，士曰「吾师也」，公亦爱其民而子之，乐与其士而弟子之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312898_comment'></div>县务虽甚烦剧，必时诣学与生徒接，始月书季考，砺术业，始立小学，迪童蒙，无小无大，日讲《论语》、《中庸》而诲以微旨，凡经子厚指教，为文皆有法，士习新美，文风丕畅，邑人士仿郡庠生祠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312898_comment'></div>先是，累大比不荐一人，复有齿贤书者，延钱君益长于学，遂登儒科，亦教化绪效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312898_comment'></div>盖公以道为己任，尹一邑则欲行于一邑，如明道先生扶沟兴学故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312898_comment'></div>他日大其用，以斯道觉斯民，使天下皆在道化中，即百里规模之充也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312898_comment'></div>某弱冠游芹泮，公期待之独厚，且尝至是邑撰杖屦，行黉舍，敬识其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312898_comment'></div>公名巨川，字东甫，尝中异科云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312898_comment'></div>淳祐四年二月朔，门人朝请郎直秘阁李昴英记<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312898_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1312898'>者：原脱，据《广州府志》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1312898_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1312898'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1312898_0'>⑴ 《文溪集》卷一。又见光绪《广州府志》卷一○二，《广东文徵》卷五五。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1312898_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年2月</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：跋魏鹤山赠医者曾贯诗。跋魏鹤山题尹商卿自信斋诗。<div id='poem_1312871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋魏鹤山赠医者曾贯诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312871")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312871'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312871'>宋清氏以子厚传之闻，姜大中以转物翁词之著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312871_comment'></div>二医皆工已疾，而不祈人之酬者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312871_comment'></div>长洲曾君客五羊，大书其门曰：「病且贫者诊乎我药施之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312871_comment'></div>是不忝鹤山赠句矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312871_comment'></div>淳祐甲辰仲春。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1312871_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋魏鹤山题尹商卿自信斋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312872")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312872'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312872'>伊川先生曰：「孔孟之门人不敢信己而信其师之说」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312872_comment'></div>朱文公曰：「信者真知其理之如此，而无毫发之疑也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312872_comment'></div>尹君试思之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1312872_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年3月1日</a>　在广州。有文。作品：广帅方右史行乡饮酒记。<div id='poem_1312897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>广帅方右史行乡饮酒记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年3月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312897")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312897'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312897'>田复井，民必棼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312897_comment'></div>战复车，卒必奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312897_comment'></div>古之泥，今之弊，固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312897_comment'></div>若夫乡饮酒，昔人岁时讲之常，尚贤而人趋善，先齿而人兴逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312897_comment'></div>俗以懿，世道以升，此礼更千万世，当如一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312897_comment'></div>人情往往乐简仍陋，非有害而惮，非小补而忽，迂之曰「理军市焉用彼」，苛之曰「起伏烦碎将难行」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312897_comment'></div>力回古风于二千馀年之后，岂易事耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312897_comment'></div>方公大琮之镇南服也，一年政优，二年化周，将古饮其州，命宾佐日在泮与领袖士讨论之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312897_comment'></div>林君公琰出一编曰：「此某人近岁行于泉者，足證也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312897_comment'></div>余君震、洪君天锡取其本，参以《仪礼》颇不合，共质之公，公曰：「吾从周」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312897_comment'></div>于是议始定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312897_comment'></div>宏纲细节，必考必据，间一二从时宜，而可以谊起，人习之咸说，未旬而熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312897_comment'></div>谋宾介，得顾君梅、陈君应辰，僎则常平使者王公铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312897_comment'></div>愚何人斯，而俾赘僎，以德凉齿劣，辞不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312897_comment'></div>乃二月十有二日质明，凡在位者颙其幅巾，粲其深衣，大带垂垂，方屦几几，以次即其席如植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312897_comment'></div>群喙一默，惟献者、酢者、酬者、执其事者交际应接，翼如襜如，莫不舂颂中度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312897_comment'></div>罍洗也、尊勺也、爵觯也、笾豆俎也，样上世而新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312897_comment'></div>就歌瑟堂，廉笙钟磬在下，间合铿鍧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312897_comment'></div>夫人目盛容，耳正音，油然心之良，驩然情之真，自以为身苍姬之元，而无昌黎不及揖逊其间之恨，盛矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312897_comment'></div>主人拜凡七十有奇，爵于上篚焉，取于东荣焉，洗于尊前焉，实于席前焉，授与其他，进退升降无算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312897_comment'></div>手献宾主人之党二百三十人，辩又疑立观二百三十人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312897_comment'></div>旅酬辩既彻俎，始膝席座以燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312897_comment'></div>漏过三十刻，强有力者犹不胜，公静专肃庄，以至送于庠门，曾不少懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312897_comment'></div>礼仪三百，威仪三千，所以行之者一，积诚定力也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312897_comment'></div>礼成，诸友合词以请曰：「吾乡乡饮酒百年几见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312897_comment'></div>乾道间龚庄敏尝行之，惜纪载脱遗，虽宿辈不可得而闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312897_comment'></div>公一循去圣之仪制，非碣其大略，来者将安稽？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312897_comment'></div>子与行礼焉，此笔宜属之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312897_comment'></div>予因告之曰：「夫礼者天理之节文，学者所以立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312897_comment'></div>平居视听言动，一之或非，是先失其恭敬之本，而物欲得以乘之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312897_comment'></div>一旦动容周旋于广众中，必周章失措，微之不可掩，于此可以观其人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312897_comment'></div>原其初心，以众人自恕，谓若昔圣人非可学而至，故自弃至此，亦可哀已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312897_comment'></div>今师帅蒐讲旷典，服古、器古、乐古，岂徒崇美名，侈美观，要使乡人士君子秉古心，行古道，不睹不闻之境，俨若对大宾时，己克而礼复，自然于其家雍，于其里恭，于其国也忠，无一毫愧于古，将见暴慢消，斗争息，陶一方之民，皆古观乡之效，易易盖不诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312897_comment'></div>唐人饮礼稍仿古耳，赞皇公在常，登歌降饮，人犹知劝，裴文献在宣，歌《白华》等章，且有泣者，二子亦直声，而公所学过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1312897_comment'></div>是举也，礼乐犹备，人心感发，又当何如」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1312897_comment'></div>众曰：「唯」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1312897_comment'></div>至于度数文为之详，则有编次在，此不书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1312897_comment'></div>淳祐四年三月朔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1312897_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　在广州。方大琮建“四先生祠”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1244&endYear=1244')">1244年</a>　在广州。是年，有文。作品：崔清献公行状。<div id='poem_1312909' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312909' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312909?labeling=true' target='_blank'>崔清献公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1244年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312909")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312909_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312909'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312909'>崔与之字正子，增城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312909_comment'></div>家贫，力学自奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312909_comment'></div>先广士有当试成均者，率惮远不行，公毅然勇往，既中选，朝夕肄业，足迹未尝至廛市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312909_comment'></div>礼部奏名廷策，极言宫闱，皆人所难言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312909_comment'></div>擢乙科，广人由胄监取第者自公始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312909_comment'></div>历浔州司法、淮西检法官，皆有守法持正之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312909_comment'></div>改秩，宰建昌新城，素号难治，公始至，岁适大歉，民有强发廪者，公折其手足以徇，因请自劾，守大异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312909_comment'></div>开禧用兵，军需苛急，公悉以县帑收市，一毫不取于民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312909_comment'></div>和籴令下，公依时直躬自交，受民自概，不扰而办，为诸邑最，赵漕使希怿令诸邑视以为法，且特荐于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312909_comment'></div>他司相继论荐，时相欲留中，公不就。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312909_comment'></div>通判邕州，荐者咸以为讶，勉公使留，公不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312909_comment'></div>诸公申其请，有旨与在内升擢差遣，公抗章控避，乞俟满而后受，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312909_comment'></div>邕守武人，惟苛刻，御禁卒无状，相率为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312909_comment'></div>公时摄宾阳，闻变亟归，叛者将拥门拒之，公疾驰以入，执首乱者戮之，纵其徒不问，阖郡帖然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312909_comment'></div>擢守宾阳，提点广西刑狱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312909_comment'></div>甫建台，遍历所部二十五州，大率皆荒寂之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312909_comment'></div>朱崖隔在海外，异时未尝识使者威仪，公至，父老骇异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312909_comment'></div>诸郡县供帐之类，一切不受，兵吏不给券，携缗钱自随，计日给之，停车决遣，无顷刻暇，奖廉劾贪，多所刺举，风采震动，召除金部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312909_comment'></div>属金人南奔，边声震恐，淮东密迩故汴，朝廷谋将帅，难其人，除公直宝谟阁、知扬州，安抚淮东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312909_comment'></div>公言边衅已开，相持六年，凡所措置，大抵虚文从事，宜择守将，集民兵以固基业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312909_comment'></div>除公工部侍郎，寻加焕章阁待制、知成都府、本路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312909_comment'></div>公言实边斯可安边，益州为四路心腹，惟恃钱谷厚于他郡，军兴帑庾告匮，宜厚储积，以壮边陲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312909_comment'></div>拜疏即行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312909_comment'></div>初，安丙檄西夏夹攻金人，不克，敌乘胜数入边，蜀大扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312909_comment'></div>丙薨，公便宜度剑以镇关表，除公制置使，尽护西蜀之师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312909_comment'></div>西北二国合从攻凤翔，叩凤州，借粮于我，公条画事宜，密授诸将随宜酬答，誊榜谕陕西五路遗黎，俾筑坞自固，倚我军为声援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312909_comment'></div>建言成都滩濑险远，艰于漕运，立运米常格奏行之，自是兵皆足食，蜀赖以全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312909_comment'></div>五年丐归，除礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312909_comment'></div>公轻舟出峡，径归五羊，自是不复出矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312909_comment'></div>筑室所居之西偏，扁「菊坡」，刻韩魏公「老圃秋容淡，黄花晚节香」之句于门塾，盖雅志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312909_comment'></div>公之门无杂宾，连帅部使者时候其门，岁仅一再见，未尝一问外事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312909_comment'></div>端平乙未二月，摧锋叛兵自惠阳拥众扣州城，郡守曾治凤宵遁，官吏群造里第，请公登城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312909_comment'></div>公肩舆至，开谕祸福，又遣门人李昴英、杨汪中缒城亲谕之，其徒俯伏听命，咸欲释甲以归，而倡谋者黠甚，以尝害博罗令，惧不免，相率遁去，入据古端州以自固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312909_comment'></div>俄有旨，依旧端明殿学士、广东经略安抚使兼知广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1312909_comment'></div>公即家治事，区处条画，揣摩调度，动中事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1312909_comment'></div>召兵四集，贼一战不支，聚其众于苦竹岭，穷蹙乞降，公命分隶降卒于诸军，而戮其桀黠者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1312909_comment'></div>俄拜参知政事，八辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1312909_comment'></div>踰年，拜右丞相，上遣中使促召，命守帅彭铉劝请，又命郎官李昴英衔命而至，逊辞凡十三疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1312909_comment'></div>上知公志不可回，诏即家条上时政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1312909_comment'></div>公手疏数万言，上皆欣纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1312909_comment'></div>家藏御札七通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1312909_comment'></div>有《文集》若干卷，其文明白谨严，家大酉书其端曰：「东海北海天下老，亦有盍归西伯时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1312909_comment'></div>白麻不能起南海，千载一人非公谁」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1312909_comment'></div>公善知人，平生荐引惟游似、洪咨夔、林略、魏了翁、李性传、程公许，后皆为公辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1312909_comment'></div>公尝度剑阁，留题词「蒲涧清泉白石，怪我旧盟寒里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1312909_comment'></div>人采其语，立公生祠于其地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1312909_comment'></div>及薨，赠太师，谥清献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1312909_comment'></div>初，公持节广右，见于施行者，维扬倅高惟肖锓梓曰《崔公岭海便民榜》，珠崖之人又编次其罢行扰民之政，曰《崔公海外澄清录》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1312909_comment'></div>在蜀人绘公像于仙游阁，与张忠定咏、赵清献抃并祠，号为三贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1312909_comment'></div>淳祐甲辰，广帅方大琮祠公与张文献九龄于学，号为二献。</div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1312909_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='afbb866691a346cda07e93c7339948a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("afbb866691a346cda07e93c7339948a2");'><span id='afbb866691a346cda07e93c7339948a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1250')">1247-1250年</a>，47-50岁</div><div id='afbb866691a346cda07e93c7339948a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：重修南海志序。书方右史请田知白作濂堂宾书后。方帅山判序。广州天庆观衆妙堂东坡井泉铭。<div id='poem_1312850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重修南海志序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312850")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312850'>志州之土地风气，莫先于表其产之良，以矜式生乎后之士，此一书大纲领也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312850_comment'></div>唐贤相起炎方者三，曰韶之张，曰日南之姜，最后得刘瞻于湟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312850_comment'></div>是时闽聚犹未有此，然皆奇拔于支郡筦府，以广名甚大，山伟海钜，秀灵鸠凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312850_comment'></div>又迟三四百载，菊坡翁始名在白麻，卧龙蒲涧之阿，勤天使走半万里莫能致，古未有命之相不屑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312850_comment'></div>高风全节，可兴百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312850_comment'></div>是邦宜有纪载以俟太史氏，而久焉犹缺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312850_comment'></div>帅方公大琮檄张君雷震曰：「邱聚不修，且四十年矣，郡文学尔职，盍讨论润色之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312850_comment'></div>乃视故府，延问老成人，分授以凡例，使各以其见闻述，然后合而参订是正焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312850_comment'></div>壅疏漏袽，诞去实存，又布之众，使疵瑕咸以为精当乃已，南国一大典，获寓目其成，何幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312850_comment'></div>余何敢涉笔其间乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312850_comment'></div>惟广素号富饶，年来浸不逮昔，而文风彪然日以张，虽蕉阜桄林之墟，蛎田蟹窟之屿，皆渠渠斋庐，币良师以玉，其子弟弦歌琤相闻，挟艺待试上都者数甚啬，每连联登名与中州等，惜人士重于簦笈远游，所以发其身秖乡举一途，故仕进者鲜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312850_comment'></div>虽然中天地而立，为世所珍，必有卓然殊于流俗者，穷达不论也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312850_comment'></div>匹夫匹妇以一行称于乡，皆可书，或高显通贵，而泯沦无闻，幢节来南，前后凡几，清名美政，照图牒有几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312850_comment'></div>使仕此而州志之观，其孰无强为善之心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312850_comment'></div>亦扶持世教一助也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312850_comment'></div>若曰山川之扁，兵赋之额，鸟兽草木之名而已耳，焉用志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312850_comment'></div>淳祐七年四月朔，职方氏李昴英序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1312850_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312895' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312895' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312895?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书方右史请田知白作濂泉堂宾书后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312895")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312895_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312895'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312895'>是邦老成人，无踰田知白者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312895_comment'></div>闻其壮即厌科举，专志理学，使领袖书生为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312895_comment'></div>知白长余三十岁，有疑必就质焉，而不敢友也，因从阙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1312895_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312851' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312851' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312851?labeling=true' target='_blank'>方帅山判序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312851")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312851_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312851'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312851'>吾儒本领在所学，而发用在所笔，心正则笔正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312851_comment'></div>平居辩经疑，破众史百氏误，以祛天下后世惑，此笔也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312851_comment'></div>其至外服则锄恶束奸，恤窭伸枉，片言分两造之曲直，此笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312851_comment'></div>时有用舍，用有内外，而所学所志无不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312851_comment'></div>方公藩峤南，晨出厅事，吏拥连牍牛腰然，森立庭下，次第而进，不竟不已，晏且暮不知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312851_comment'></div>落笔累千言，原情据法，必曲必尽，虽刑之夺之无怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312851_comment'></div>第一义则厚人伦，美风俗，故道化孚畅，所部大治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312851_comment'></div>一判出，佐属争手抄，久焉所编钜，乃汇分而梓，于寄来者稽焉，知学校、兵防、财计之本末，与炎人之情伪习尚，能推行其说，流惠益远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312851_comment'></div>公治广之懿固不专在此，而五年目力心思，大概聚于此，泯没可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312851_comment'></div>判可称者唐香山，我朝武溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312851_comment'></div>然拘牵俪对，或未能尽写其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312851_comment'></div>公之判斡旋顿挫，只字不苟，真可为吏师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312851_comment'></div>世方纤巧诗词，新集捷出在在有，真可酱瓿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312851_comment'></div>此刻皆及物实，功不腐宜哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1312851_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在广州。有词。作品：贺新郎（绣谷流明帜）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　在广州。广帅方大琮卒，有祭文。作品：祭广帅右史方鐡菴大琮公文。<div id='poem_1312914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312914?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭广帅右史方铁庵大琮公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312914")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312914'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312914'>厥今人望，若晨星稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312914_comment'></div>公老远播，天复夺之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312914_comment'></div>岂惟广人之悲，海内善类，盖莫不歔欷也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312914_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312914_comment'></div>公之学探圣门之微，公之文根理窟而奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312914_comment'></div>静者其性，而敬以持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312914_comment'></div>暄日霁风，接物怡怡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312914_comment'></div>见义勇为，铁石不移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312914_comment'></div>敢言动天，无愧拾遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312914_comment'></div>使部其乡，肯故人私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312914_comment'></div>盖海旂幢，前谁五期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312914_comment'></div>精神筋力，毕竭于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312914_comment'></div>器古乐成，幅巾深衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312914_comment'></div>乡饮凡三，动中礼仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312914_comment'></div>斋庐闳闳，书阁巍巍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312914_comment'></div>玉女青衿，贤哉帅师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312914_comment'></div>牍累千言，判墨淋漓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312914_comment'></div>两造息争，晓之片辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312914_comment'></div>雪轸尔寒，荒恤尔饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312914_comment'></div>手拊遐氓，父母其慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312914_comment'></div>崇堂大榭，辟圃东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312914_comment'></div>杖屦婆娑，民共敖嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312914_comment'></div>突兀军门，雄视南维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312914_comment'></div>库曰备安，贮缗不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312914_comment'></div>为此州千年计，而百废必治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312914_comment'></div>子产之仁，校人犹欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312914_comment'></div>孝肃之明，吏计得施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312914_comment'></div>人知公心，如玉无疵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312914_comment'></div>大书连篇，几德政碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312914_comment'></div>万人香火，在在生祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312914_comment'></div>盖信之久，德之深，不待其去而后思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312914_comment'></div>诏徙洪都，将以公归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312914_comment'></div>素无病恼，一卧不支。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312914_comment'></div>语音朗然，易箦之时，面貌如生，卒袭之尸，所养又可知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1312914_comment'></div>某畴昔尝寮，今巢一枝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1312914_comment'></div>肺肝不隔，真切相规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1312914_comment'></div>商评古今，竟日麈挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1312914_comment'></div>公不可作，何所质疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1312914_comment'></div>酒落涕俱，世少子期。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1312914_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　在广州。广帅方大琮卒，又有祭文。作品：又路祭方右史。<div id='poem_1312915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312915?labeling=true' target='_blank'>又路祭方右史文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312915")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312915'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312915'>輀车东浮兮，黄水之湾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312915_comment'></div>倾城挽送兮，积涕回澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312915_comment'></div>鱼龙泣护，海山惨颜，恶人多寿兮，贤者不使之生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312915_comment'></div>还天不可问兮，时事愈艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312915_comment'></div>十年缔交兮，相照胆肝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312915_comment'></div>色笑若平生兮，梦寐之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312915_comment'></div>罗浮之约付渺茫兮，冷月空山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312915_comment'></div>想像苍虬于炎洲兮，一酹招魂。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312915_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　在广州。广帅方大琮卒，挽诗。作品：挽右史方铁菴诗三首（其一）挽右史方铁菴诗三首（其二）挽右史方铁菴诗三首（其三）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：别陈霆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年5月</a>　在广州。徐清叟帅广，有诗。作品：迎广帅徐意一大叅五首（其一）迎广帅徐意一大叅五首（其二）迎广帅徐意一大叅五首（其三）迎广帅徐意一大叅五首（其四）迎广帅徐意一大叅五首（其五）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年11月</a>　在广州。除知赣州，不赴，有辞状。作品：辞免知赣州状。<div id='poem_1312815' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312815' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312815?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免知赣州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312815")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312815_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312815'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312815'>照对某淳祐七年十二月初九日准当年十一月空日尚书省劄子，备据某状辞免，缴回差知赣州省劄，十一月三日，三省同奉圣旨不允，并元省劄付某者，殊渥仍颁，微躬无措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312815_comment'></div>某切谓荣宠乃人情之同欲，威令宜臣子之钦承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312815_comment'></div>矧闲废而得州，合驰驱而徇国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312815_comment'></div>伏念某最凉其分，不竞于才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312815_comment'></div>咸谓之迂，非剸裁之敏手；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312815_comment'></div>而有斯病，由忧惧之熏心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312815_comment'></div>字对眼以如遮，事转头而随忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312815_comment'></div>曾是可当于剧任，冒然缴纳于除书，虽不加以方命之诛，犹例待以具文之逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312815_comment'></div>量己莫裨于世用，吁天更积于衷忱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312815_comment'></div>控告庙堂，奏彻旒冕，悯此柳蒲之脆质，许其香火于真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312815_comment'></div>二千石起家之除，不为弃物；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312815_comment'></div>一再伛循墙之避，庶附全人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312815_comment'></div>所有省劄二道，寄留广州军资库，未敢祗受，须至申闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1312815_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年12月2日</a>　在广州。除福建提刑，有辞状,不准。作品：辞免除福建提刑状。<div id='poem_1312816' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312816' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312816?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除福建提刑状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1247年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312816")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312816_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312816'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312816'>照会某淳祐八年正月二十二日准淳祐七年十二月二日，三省同奉圣旨，李某依旧直秘阁，除福建提刑，劄付某者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312816_comment'></div>异恩沓至，小己若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312816_comment'></div>伏念某起自单寒，最为绵薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312816_comment'></div>樗栎散材之无用，岂适时宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312816_comment'></div>草茅习气之未除，易与物忤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312816_comment'></div>内徒污于班缀，外何有于民庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312816_comment'></div>侥荣颇越于分涯，未老已成于衰證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312816_comment'></div>怔忡多忘，视听难真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312816_comment'></div>一障承流，尚虑驽疲之弗称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312816_comment'></div>列城折狱，自怜鼯技以奚堪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312816_comment'></div>敢贪斧绣之荣，懔有针毡之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312816_comment'></div>莫裨国事，徒速官刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312816_comment'></div>仰祈宰路之奏陈，特畀祠庭之闲散。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312816_comment'></div>倘必待其旷败而后加汰斥，孰若察其真切而早赐存全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312816_comment'></div>退处山林，庶可疗采薪之病；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312816_comment'></div>稍迟岁月，不敢辞蹈刃之难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312816_comment'></div>所有省劄寄留广州军资库，未敢祗受，须至申闻者。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1312816_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在广州。又改知漳州，辞，不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在广州。是年，有诗。作品：酌别张子元二首（其一）酌别张子元二首（其二）送张子元班见。寿张新班。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年1月22日</a>　在广州。诏依旧直秘阁，除福建提刑，有文。作品：辞免除福建提刑状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：韶石说送曲江赵广文。题三衢陈大经诗卷。跋邓运判柞行实。<div id='poem_1312843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312843?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韶石说送曲江赵广文序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312843")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312843'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312843'>韶，尽善之乐也，以名州，嘉矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312843_comment'></div>名之则昉于唐初，去舜之时如此其远也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312843_comment'></div>山有异状石，耆老相传尝于此九成焉，故石之形肖之，其说甚荒唐无稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312843_comment'></div>粤岭秦始通，南巡狩故未必至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312843_comment'></div>然圣人声教之溥，如日月所照，霜露所坠，粤当舜之世，独不在舜之天地中乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312843_comment'></div>甚矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312843_comment'></div>圣人之德，感人之深且久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312843_comment'></div>后乎舜千有馀岁，季札观乐，三叹不已，夫子闻遗音，肉食焉而不味，至于今又千有馀岁，而石其思，庙其依，常隐然在人心，舜何以得此于州之人，州之人何以不能忘于舜也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312843_comment'></div>孰谓州之人非其遗民乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312843_comment'></div>则此石特人心感触之一机，不必致疑可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312843_comment'></div>教授赵君崇禋既模南海礼乐器，以文丁奠，且将乐于有虞氏之祠，以实是州之名，好古敏以求之者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312843_comment'></div>舜何人也，有为者亦若是，此当求之于金石丝竹之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312843_comment'></div>赵君淑诸生而古其心，必有道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312843_comment'></div>淳祐八年二月朔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1312843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1312843'><span class='label'>按：</span>《文溪集》卷一二。又见光绪《曲江县志》卷四；《广东文献初集》卷三，民国油印本《广东文徵》卷二五。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1312843_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1312886' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312886' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312886?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题三衢陈大经诗卷</a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年8月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312886")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312886_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312886'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312886'>陈君自号岫云，所以寄萧闲之趣，非以是状其诗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312886_comment'></div>而澹乎物表，纳宇宙之大于胸次，吐之成韵，自然清绝不尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312886_comment'></div>君诗多态度，蔼蔼春空云，必有赏音如昌黎翁者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312886_comment'></div>淳祐八年八月八日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312886_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312865' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312865' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312865?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋邓运判柞行实<span class='inlineComment2'>（始兴人）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年8月20日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312865")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312865_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312865'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312865'>予闻耆老言桂漕邓公平难事，英气奥谋不在杜杞下，老桧欲啖以美官，使摧残谪客，则崖然正色拒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312865_comment'></div>士志于立功，少定力，公则将之以学，故能不为势利所移，高广于上书布衣中，识拔南方一杰，可谓无遗才矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312865_comment'></div>淳祐八年八月二十日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1312865_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年9月</a>　在广州。致书臣相郑清之，乞免知赣州。作品：上郑臣相书。<div id='poem_1312827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上郑丞相书<span class='inlineComment2'>（淳祐八年九月乞免知赣州）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312827")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312827'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312827'>昴英楷题既襞，不敢琐碎仪式，恐贻溷渎之谴，首乞钧照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312827_comment'></div>昴英疏远之踪，狂迂之性，不识事体，沙斥固宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312827_comment'></div>自归三径，杜门扫轨，诵习故书，求以克去气质之偏，获逭谪徙，已为万幸，安敢作荣进梦！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312827_comment'></div>忽叨误渥，予郡起家，圣天子乾坤同量，不弃蝼蚁之微，庙堂包荒，不遗葑菲之贱，得之如惊，感深以愧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312827_comment'></div>自合奔走奉职，少见寸尺，以赎往愆，实缘一春行役，冲雨湿，感风邪，百疾交攻，精力全衰，偷安泉石间，尚可以徐徐疗治，倘冒焉当繁剧之任，必至败缺，不惟身计之误，而误国之罪大矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312827_comment'></div>心之精微，尽在免牍，谨录副申呈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312827_comment'></div>五羊去天四千里，驶辈一往返，动是三阅月，而虎城重地，宜亟选长才，所以不避诛殛，缴回省劄者，盖欲一时而遂所请，非特为身计，实为公尔计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312827_comment'></div>欲望钧慈为之密启于冕旒之前，庶几小臣真切之悃，获彻崇高之听，收回成命，畀以丛祠，使进退稍安，不得罪于物议，其荣过于二千石多矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312827_comment'></div>此身未填沟壑，他日尚能蹈刀锯鼎镬，以报国恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312827_comment'></div>干冒钧严，不胜战惕之至！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　在广州。赵汝腾有“三老八士”之荐。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1248&endYear=1248')">1248年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：与秘书徐霖札子。题刘浔州必成三分集。与广帅徐意一荐僧祖中书。和徐意一韵赠宝积中空山。<div id='poem_1312828' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312828' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312828?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与秘书徐霖劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（淳祐八年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312828")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312828_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312828'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312828'>某去腊束担出六和塔，朝士送者才四，执事其一也，相与促膝攒眉，语至暮而后出，别后忽十阅月，怀贤耿耿，一食息不能忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312828_comment'></div>四千里跋涉，春晏方抵弊庐，杜门扫轨，一字不敢出门，故于畏友亦一例似疏绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312828_comment'></div>迩者耸闻大声疾呼之疏，上拂衣径归，天子洒翰，大臣联札，清班追挽，竟不能回天马之驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312828_comment'></div>向来首摇冰山，已立罗浮四千丈之上，此举前无古人，又在祝融峰九千丈之巅矣，卓乎高哉，不可跂而及也已，敬叹敬叹！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312828_comment'></div>某婆娑三径，熟复故书，粗得静味，忽误渥予郡起家，乃与重名同一除书，厕秽形于玉侧，颇觉羞愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312828_comment'></div>圣天子天地其量，超轶古昔，恩宠殊常，本不敢控辞，私念平日受教菊坡公，讲明出处最不草草，深惧得罪清议，为先师辱，故以真实之悃，写之免章，切度公朝必见察，可以遂所请，凡可以开发者幸不鄙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312828_comment'></div>相去三千馀里，无从握手倾倒，倚风惘惘，乞为伟器自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312828_comment'></div>不宣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312828_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题刘浔州必成三分集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312883")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312883'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312883'>嘉熙丁酉秋，余被命衡文贡闱，右科中得一奇士，揭之解首，则刘君必成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312883_comment'></div>明年，君廷对魁其伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312883_comment'></div>又十年，以清浔使君寓南海，始熟其标致论议，竞爽可人，与其所为文不异，而吟尤工，豪逸雅澹，兼众体，题所编曰《三分》，取东坡戏郭功甫语也，谦退不自足如此，进未易涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312883_comment'></div>虽然，世有擅八义之才，而他无可书者，器识先而文艺后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312883_comment'></div>立身行己，当如前辈所谓八九分人，推以及物，必宽之一分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312883_comment'></div>君所学所志，盖有余所期望者，不但进于诗而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312883_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312829' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312829' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312829?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与广帅徐意一荐僧祖中书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1248年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312829")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312829_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312829'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312829'>某数年不到罗浮，梦寐见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312829_comment'></div>近招宝积僧祖中来，出瓶中卓锡泉烹石楼新茗，共谈山中事，清风忽起坐间，飘飘然如行飞云顶也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312829_comment'></div>某岁在甲辰，两游罗浮，至必住旬日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312829_comment'></div>山广大深远不可穷，而山中人绝少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312829_comment'></div>道人则有王宁素，年八十馀，碧瞳炯然照人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312829_comment'></div>头陀则有祖演，年高过之，发色如黄金，僧可语者，仅仅斯人耳，此大梦德因之子而克肖者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312829_comment'></div>将辞归中阁，必欲识意一而后去，渠无他求，必有异乎人之求者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312829_comment'></div>风雨如许，政斋阁焚香静坐时，试延之前，使呈露所蕴，必不能谩具眼，得闻侍郎一声，归山林作话柄，窃度其所求不过如此而已，进之退之，惟所以命。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312829_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。上书广帅邱迪嚞治盗，全活者数百人。作品：与广权帅邱迪嚞治盗书。<div id='poem_1312830' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312830' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312830?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与广权帅邱迪哲治盗书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312830")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312830_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312830'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312830'>某晦藏林谷，不敢与闻户外事，每荷庞汉阳先候之廑，且惧杜周甫寒蝉之诮，有闻而不以告，终愧于心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312830_comment'></div>民吾同胞也，况父母之邦之民乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312830_comment'></div>方此上下疑惧之时，某傥以利害不切己而不知恤，桑梓之人交责以义，无以自立于父母之邦矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312830_comment'></div>夫治盗固贵于严，尤贵于审，惟非盗或遭横戮，而真盗未必能获，此贼盗所以滋多也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312830_comment'></div>前乎尝闻途人之言曰：某人以姓名同而捕，某人以盗贼之亲属而捕，几人善良也，亦皆捕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312830_comment'></div>未几，则某人脔矣，某人枭矣，某人截手足而死矣，心甚悼之，而悔不先以此闻彻足下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312830_comment'></div>伯仁由我而死之，念至今不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312830_comment'></div>日来所闻，又有甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312830_comment'></div>盖官司捉贼，不容不倚办于隅总，而为隅总者类皆小人，不识道理，但知凭威势为奸利，安知人命之为重！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312830_comment'></div>往往半公半私，以快其所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312830_comment'></div>或宿怨之未偿，或厚需之未厌，或党与之所仇，阴嗾使之，甚其诬捏送于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312830_comment'></div>彼觊厚赏者利于俘数之多，略不分别，躬自讯鞫，穷极惨酷，谁不承伏！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312830_comment'></div>虽分丽诸狱，然群有司非卓然自立者，未有不承望风旨，自为身谋，何敢可否于其间！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312830_comment'></div>足下以疾恶之心，视已成之牍，则皆死有馀罪，有非其实情，足下乌得而知之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312830_comment'></div>利归于小人，谤归于足下，使足下知之，必不肯轻于笔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312830_comment'></div>自清远凶徒日就擒获，则足下之功亦伟矣，必不藉此区区数辈以张功状，非通徭而为通徭，非贼而诬以贼，岂足下之本心哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312830_comment'></div>今士窃议于途，什什伍伍，颦蹙私语，而某于朔旦固尝面言其略，既而闻用事者有遂非之意，恐足下竟为憸巧转移，草菅斯民，亏足下之盛德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312830_comment'></div>某连日思之，食不下咽，寝不安席，私念此身非侥倖一官，家在城市，安保此祸之不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312830_comment'></div>惟视人犹己之心，噤不一语，安乎故，盛服焚香，吁天而布此札，稍有一毫私心，天地鬼神其诛殛之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312830_comment'></div>惟足下是非之间，审之又审，谨之又谨，与其杀不辜，宁失不经，使平民免于屠戮，于门之阴德岂易涯邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312830_comment'></div>某狂妄之言，至此极矣，不敢复有言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312830_comment'></div>若足下不以为然，而不加之意，则是邦之民，遭此厄会，某抑末如之何也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312830_comment'></div>惓惓爱助之心，惟足下其察之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1312830_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1312830'><span class='label'>按：</span>《文溪集》卷一○。又见《广东文献初集》卷三，民国油印本《广东文徵》卷一九。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1312830_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。为佥王所陷，褫阁职，有诗。作品：闻禠阁职免新任之报二首（其一）闻禠阁职免新任之报二首（其二）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：题潜守黄莲传。跋潜守治狱好生方。<div id='poem_1312877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题潜守黄连传</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312877")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312877'>雪岩潜君起传黄连，以其味苦而能愈疾，犹言忠而能救缺遗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312877_comment'></div>然苦易厌，忠易疏，古今同一病，此佳传可药天下后世，岂但体物游笔力而已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312877_comment'></div>予尝谓黄连最甘，举世莫晓，盖不适口顷刻耳，为身已安，非甘乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312877_comment'></div>物之甜人，其害有沉痼不可疗者，非苦乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312877_comment'></div>日昃不暇食，文亦劳止，终与民皆欢乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312877_comment'></div>玄宗末年，声色岂不大快意，卒不宴于蜀，明验可睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312877_comment'></div>夫君心苦、身苦、学苦、行苦，其性黄连，其气味黄连，宁自苦而欲遗世以至甘，故言尤苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312877_comment'></div>必有持是言进之上者，国脉庶其有瘳乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312877_comment'></div>唐博士《岭南贡蜜果诗》曰：「政恐无裨益，所出非和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312877_comment'></div>上林宁少此，下箸安可轻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312877_comment'></div>在惠阳作也，其忠爱深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312877_comment'></div>《黄连传》，惠阳所著二篇政堪作对。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1312877_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312878' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312878' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312878?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋潜守治狱好生方</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312878")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312878_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312878'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312878'>《治狱好生方》，雪岩潜起所制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312878_comment'></div>方所主者一，曰仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312878_comment'></div>其用有三，曰研之实，辨之白，决之早。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312878_comment'></div>余始读之，意其如世医，虽能处方，未必有真见定力，能察脉投剂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312878_comment'></div>南海值厄，运漕邱迪哲摄帅，尉陈知章摄倅，以残虐为能，以多杀为功，时号大小屠伯，虎噬蟒吞，俘平民为寇，累累血刀杌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312878_comment'></div>绣衣陈公均久知君，檄之详讯，凶人方煽威焰，胁制同列，或劝君引避可以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312878_comment'></div>君奋然曰：「人命至重，但平心睹是，己之祸福利害，在所不论」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312878_comment'></div>乃躬审问，具得情实，赖以更生者十九，与唐眉山序萧师颜明兴元狱非叛，活数十人事颇相类，人始服君有活人手，能用此方矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312878_comment'></div>既随试效，不得不广传。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312878_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：肇庆府倅王庚应平反广府帅司冤狱诗以纪其事。苦秋暑行（并序）送广东宪陈均二首（其一）送广东宪陈均二首（其二）哭清远权宰楼海司法二首（其一）哭清远权宰楼海司法二首（其二）送李路钤万入京（并序）代送邱漕迪哲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年6月25日</a>　在广州。有文。作品：题循阳通守黄必昌大学中庸讲义。<div id='poem_1312866' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312866' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312866?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题循阳通守黄必昌大学中庸讲义</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年6月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312866")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312866_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312866'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312866'>吾友黄京甫主濂堂日，沃诸生胸次以《大学》、《中庸》之味，揭宏举要，阐邃析微，探圣贤妙旨于千百载之下，取儒先绪论，蔽之片言间，体认真切处，如良画状人物，考察精密处，如历家步星气，于义理无少差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312866_comment'></div>盖渊源乎北溪，而根柢乎考亭者，为后学之益多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312866_comment'></div>京甫循循修谨人，一语不妄发，意其于二书心之身之久，不但工诵说而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312866_comment'></div>然士之讲学岂惟独善，要推以泽民利物，与上官相可否，毋有所恐惧，见义必为，行之以勇，又持此书判千里矣，勉之哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312866_comment'></div>淳祐九年六月二十五日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1312866_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。是年秋，有诗送后学。作品：秋试已近用韵勉儿辈。送次儿解试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：观入试者。再用观入试韵。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。三子志道以《春秋》领乡荐，有诗勉励。作品：送三举人（并序）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1249&endYear=1249')">1249年</a>　在广州。季弟奎英卒。有文。作品：赠香山王公。<div id='poem_1312846' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312846' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312846?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠香山王公序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1249年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312846")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312846_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312846'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312846'>先人与香山王公为莫逆交，余儿时撰杖屦，侍左右，见其情好亲密如兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312846_comment'></div>先人下世，今九年，执友凋几尽，独翁一个在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312846_comment'></div>扁舟远远入城叙契阔，余适有季弟之戚，不能欸曲陪色笑，而遽辞归，使人感慨不忍别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312846_comment'></div>翁六十有九，强健不少衰，许明年重来，必不渝此盟也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312846_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：书胡致堂叙古千文后。跋菊坡太学生时书稿。<div id='poem_1312857' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312857' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312857?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书胡致堂叙古千文后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312857")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312857_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312857'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312857'>文定胡公潜心《春秋》四十馀年，而后徐出其说，致堂其亲传，故笔削皆有法，叙古字凡千不重，虽饮席间谈笑成之，而上下数千载，关系大处包撮略尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312857_comment'></div>兴君昏主之理乱，哲佐悖臣之功罪，吾道异端之正遍，一字森严，百世确论，不但可以习童稚而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312857_comment'></div>古千文偎陋不伦，乃盛行于世俗，盖未知有此作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312857_comment'></div>其书一经朱文公表揭，遂传广帅宋公慈里两翁之里学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312857_comment'></div>两翁之学既梓之衡阳，又梓之广之泮宫，自此流布天下，人人得讽咏，有功于人心多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312857_comment'></div>南岳之高，南海之深，不泯不磨致堂之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312857_comment'></div>淳祐十年月正元日，后学李昴英书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1312857_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312863' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312863' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312863?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋菊坡太学生时书稿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年2月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312863")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312863_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312863'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312863'>此清献公初入太学，寄其友林介仲书也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312863_comment'></div>吾州去在所四千里，水浮陆驰，大约七十程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312863_comment'></div>士以补试，虽登名，犹未脱韦布也，故稍有事力者犹劳且费之，惮而尼其行，寒士又可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312863_comment'></div>公奋然间关独往，一试预选，随取高第，平生勋业名节，实贤关基之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312863_comment'></div>长短句有「人世易老」之叹，必期三年成名，而归书所云云，立志已卓然不凡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312863_comment'></div>至于述斋舍之费颇悉，闻其入京参斋时皆朋友相资助，故书报之详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312863_comment'></div>贫者士之常，公之贫有人不堪其忧者，处之甚安，所以富贵不能淫，而清白照一世也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312863_comment'></div>林介仲名介，增江老儒者，生没在公之前，后人不能宝有此纸，转落士人之家，某近始得之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312863_comment'></div>公以岁庚戌入在胶庠，庚戌而此书出，若有数然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312863_comment'></div>外侄陈某往试桥门，持此授儿子守道，守道亦就试，且婿菊坡之门，公手泽宜归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312863_comment'></div>淳祐十年二月朔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1312863_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年2月</a>　在广州。许巨川卒，有祭文。作品：祭许象州文。<div id='poem_1312912' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312912' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312912?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭许象州文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312912")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312912_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312912'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312912'>维淳祐十年岁次庚戌二月朔越祭日，门人朝散大夫李某谨以清酌，告于近故判府朝议钝斋许公先生：钝斋之学，本源一诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312912_comment'></div>文最近古，诚之著形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312912_comment'></div>政先及物，诚之流行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312912_comment'></div>问无不知，惟诚故精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312912_comment'></div>事至能应，惟诚故明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312912_comment'></div>诚则无欲，冰蘖自清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312912_comment'></div>诚则无营，轩冕甚轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312912_comment'></div>师道自任，南海横经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312912_comment'></div>曾入范模，一一玉成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312912_comment'></div>士德之深，共祠之黉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312912_comment'></div>至今朔望，罗拜于庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312912_comment'></div>弦歌东筦，课试始程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312912_comment'></div>亦崇厥祠，书阁峥嵘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312912_comment'></div>菊坡西山，皆极口称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312912_comment'></div>才可经纶，位不公卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312912_comment'></div>既踰七帙，乃仅双旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312912_comment'></div>辍俸廪士，食续贡英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312912_comment'></div>藻饰泮宫，百废并兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312912_comment'></div>米入斛减，盐出衡增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312912_comment'></div>宁捐公家，以宽远氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312912_comment'></div>曾未期月，洋乎政声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312912_comment'></div>老不废卷，细书如蝇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312912_comment'></div>斯文之厄，泰山俄倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312912_comment'></div>志未尽伸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312912_comment'></div>用未及宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312912_comment'></div>夫人惜嗟，而况诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312912_comment'></div>某少撰杖屦，早蒙旦评。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312912_comment'></div>诲犹药石，爱犹父兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312912_comment'></div>犹记厦旃，荐公姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312912_comment'></div>年貌几何，清问亲聆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312912_comment'></div>未几去国，竟负师承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312912_comment'></div>灵輀来东，酹洒涕凝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312912_comment'></div>返筑未能，何敢不铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312912_comment'></div>伏惟尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1312912_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年2月</a>　在广州。有诗挽许巨川。作品：挽钝斋先生许象州三首（其一）挽钝斋先生许象州三首（其二）挽钝斋先生许象州三首（其三）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：题彭昌诗下车録。赠怀集莫贡士。赠传神张森。<div id='poem_1312892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题彭昌诗下车录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年4月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312892")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312892'>下车而揖戴笠，此布衣交富贵毋相忘之约耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312892_comment'></div>若夫一言而善，介卿下堂，一字之工，大尹驻驭，前达之赏识，士不必旧尝半面也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312892_comment'></div>士有安穷阎而陋结驷，寄饮市而傲召轮，又曷尝汲汲焉觊贵显者之一顾盼哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312892_comment'></div>穷达不足以论士，新故不足以论交，所以意气相与，惟其人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312892_comment'></div>人如彭君昌诗所至，谁不倒屣，谁不下榻？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312892_comment'></div>帙此以谒诸公，庶几他日一邂逅，虽似乎赘视世俗所谓云萍录泛泛然，纪载则大异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312892_comment'></div>余方耕钓文溪，上效东坡雨笠曳屐，则轩渠甚适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312892_comment'></div>乘车骛荣，途者甚多矣，君必欲颓然山夫，笔其编甚矣，其迂之过我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312892_comment'></div>淳祐十年四月既望。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312892_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312845' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312845' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312845?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠怀集莫贡士序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年5月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312845")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312845_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312845'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312845'>不见莫君瑞应八年，忽叩门访，小隐留之，对荷花细酌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312845_comment'></div>因谈怀集产水晶石，莹明特异，惜吾邑无能攻治之者，列之几案，供拊玩，清寒照人，亦天成奇物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312845_comment'></div>余曰：「君亦犹是，夫一日遇良工具眼，稍加琢磋，即成美器矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312845_comment'></div>时有龙舟跃至小溪，君喜甚，举大白满引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312845_comment'></div>淳祐十年夏五月朔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1312845_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312847' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312847' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312847?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠传神张森序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1250年5月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312847")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312847_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312847'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312847'>建张材叔以能模写晦庵翁名江湖间，艺工也，而多从名公卿游，气象犹士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312847_comment'></div>非若世之庸手，但能看人颜面，弄粉墨，探理义之精微，岂不有得于公之心也哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312847_comment'></div>余曩使建，将绘公像，问孰能之者，皆首称材叔，后致之，果奇笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312847_comment'></div>别十馀年，忽来访山居，技益老，老益穷，南山数千里，逐食役役无宁岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312847_comment'></div>蜀僧之霭传神得妙，柳仲涂谓其至艺天与纤无差忒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312847_comment'></div>写太宗龙颜，天为之笑，宠荣冠一时，品题连篇，不止一仲涂，而材叔至今不遇，何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312847_comment'></div>遇不遇有命焉，归寻旧隐，集西山数老宿褒字遗子孙，足以不朽，孰谓材叔不遇哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312847_comment'></div>淳祐十年端午日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312847_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1250&endYear=1250')">1250年</a>　在广州。是年，有诗送叶耆卿试太学。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='3d9247594202495fb4e4bde6e23f9bc2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3d9247594202495fb4e4bde6e23f9bc2");'><span id='3d9247594202495fb4e4bde6e23f9bc2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1252')">1251-1252年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='3d9247594202495fb4e4bde6e23f9bc2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年11月1日</a>　在广州。冬至日有文。作品：跋节愍王公行实。<div id='poem_1312864' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312864' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312864?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋节悯王公行实</a><span class='authorDate'>（1251年11月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312864")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312864_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312864'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312864'>舍生取义，所欲有甚于生者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312864_comment'></div>平生讲之熟，故临难处之雍容，非猝然勉强能之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312864_comment'></div>敌之犯益也，节悯王公翊以议官权宜肘制置使印，收烬兵，支孤城，野战不胜，巷战又不胜，然后徐结缨而入于井，此他人之责，而身之不避，壮矣哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312864_comment'></div>先是，菊坡崔公贻之书曰：「一段冰清，万仞壁立」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312864_comment'></div>窃意公平生忠义自许，惟菊坡深期之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312864_comment'></div>其子阊募死士赴难，道遇兵，且斗且前，创甚，偶不死，今为东莞丞，遂得见公行实与守城日记，风节凛凛，使人慨慕，且三叹菊坡知人之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312864_comment'></div>淳祐辛亥冬至，文溪李昴英书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1312864_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1251&endYear=1251')">1251年</a>　在广州。是年，有词。作品：《摸鱼儿》（敞茅堂）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>，55岁</div><div id='ced3a1b519554f4eacca31087ab330c9' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在广州。有文。作品：书胡侯竹巢七思集。<div id='poem_1312882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书胡侯竹巢七思集</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312882")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312882'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312882'>细诵胡侯大学《七思》之作，迎驾谒殿之篇，其纲领与君之仁所以教育我，师之道所以作成我，功与天地并，盖终身受其赐，如之何勿思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312882_comment'></div>侯去璧水几年，而卷卷然形之声诗，视世之豢富贵而忘齑盐者大径庭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312882_comment'></div>兹牧千里，将行夫子之言，以泽天子之民，推广其所思，则天下有溺者、饥者，皆在吾念虑中，侯必勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312882_comment'></div>宝祐三年七月二十三日，南海李昴英书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>归广州，隐居羊城文溪之上，著书行于世，无复仕进。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>归广州。是年，有诗。作品：题罗浮沖虚观化缘疏。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='332f0b1c520c4e5c91b983d46baf9f14_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。春，作诗赠曾士倬。作品：赠曾士倬用许广文韵。<br /><a href="javascript:
