ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。捐资建海珠慈度寺，王野为题寺额。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。诏除端明殿学士，佥书枢密院事，不赴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。御书“久远”“文溪”“向阳堂”赐之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：司法曾子美新第荣归欲得余诗不敢效世俗谀语二首（其一）司法曾子美新第荣归欲得余诗不敢效世俗谀语二首（其二）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：寿安院记。<div id='poem_1312906' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312906' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312906?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寿安院记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1256年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312906")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312906_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312906'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312906'>天地之大德生而已，所以无终穷，生意不息而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312906_comment'></div>凡物囿形，其数之自然；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312906_comment'></div>惨舒，其气之使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312906_comment'></div>彭殇椿菌，固不容强齐，亦各正性命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312906_comment'></div>大君位乎中，妙赞化育，分群有司，代天工，要使生意流布，充满覆载间，无一物不得其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312906_comment'></div>国朝置福田院恤穷疾，与天地同一好生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312906_comment'></div>常平仓专使领为凶荒疾疫设，将以救民病，而或者反以政事病民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312906_comment'></div>今天子轸远方元元，选物望民庸兼者畀，右司刘公、仓氏节公一意推广皇泽，进耆老诹之曰：「赋过重痏吾民欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312906_comment'></div>役不均瘠吾民欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312906_comment'></div>官吏饕脧吾民欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312906_comment'></div>追呼数恼吾民欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312906_comment'></div>豪龂椎剥，吾民郁不吐欤」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312906_comment'></div>闻一事系戚休，亟罢行不终日，南人如解沉疴积痼，豁然苏快，无复愁嗟，公犹以为未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312906_comment'></div>广，山宽海钜，岚雾散泄，故无瘴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312906_comment'></div>土饶醲鲜，细人恣属厌，亦易疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312906_comment'></div>鳏寡孤独之穷，川浮陆负之贾，驰书传檄之价，才病于主家，旅馆则畏其累己，迫遣之，往往转徙闾巷，虽受病本轻，而不粒不剂，且风且露，困顿久必僵，厢逻又视为奇货，重诛求于死，所为邦人害最大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312906_comment'></div>公恻然效东坡在杭蓄钱粮作病坊故事，乃相爽垲址于威远门之内，穹堂闳闳，严祷祠香火，干僧其左，医局其右，修廊渠渠，对辟十室，可容十人，男东女西，界限有别，病无依者以告，随得入，诊必工，药必良，食必精，烹煎责两，童缁必恪，日欲闻所苦重轻，课医之效，募夫妇愿俱庸者共凡役，庖斯整，湢斯洁，百尔器用色色具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312906_comment'></div>奄奄无聊赖之人忽处广厦，适眠飧所需如意，顿使神醒气伸，居养所移半药力，既康强，则资之归，脱不可疗，则歛瘗如法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312906_comment'></div>租收之田，赢取之库，所入足以当所出，画为成规，可行之悠久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312906_comment'></div>外峙崇门曰寿安，颜其院，因人情所欲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312906_comment'></div>扶曳来居无虚日，全活甚众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312906_comment'></div>人病之者既能厝之安，天病之者亦欲拯之生，公之心无愧于两间，无负于吾君矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312906_comment'></div>夫人为三才之一，仁人心也与天地心本不二，如果核中有仁，生意在焉，恻隐其端，不特发见于孺子将入井时，虽草木禽兽之微，萎瘁不得宁其生，亦悯焉动念，病柏病橘，病马病鸱，杜诗韩笔且不遗，而况于民吾同胞乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312906_comment'></div>苟其位其力可以利众庶，而呻吟叫呼在吾境，若不闻，良心安在哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312906_comment'></div>公可以为仁人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312906_comment'></div>盖元祐相国忠肃公其六世祖也，家学源流，有所自来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312906_comment'></div>公名震孙，字长翁，渤海人。</div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1312906_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：同刘朔斋游白云寺二首（其一）同刘朔斋游白云寺二首（其二）同刘朔斋游蒲涧谒菊坡祠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有词。作品：水调歌头（万顷黄湾口）满江红（人似梅花）菩萨蛮（云山叠叠双眸短）贺新郎（世羡官高大）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：山行。碧霄。白云登阁。灵洲。游峡山和东坡韵。峡山全清阁。登峡山疾风甚雨。峡山飞来殿。景泰寺。云泉亭。后峒月溪寺二首（其一）后峒月溪寺二首（其二）北山证果寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1256&endYear=1256')">1256年</a>　在广州。有词。作品：摸鱼儿（晓风痴）贺新郎（细与黄花说）水调歌头（郭外足幽胜）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年3月3日</a>　在广州。有文。作品：增城新创贡士库记。<div id='poem_1312899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>增城新创贡士库记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312899")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312899'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312899'>曲江以文献重，增城以清献重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312899_comment'></div>清献起陋巷，取巍科，至于今六十年矣，其间踵名第不乏人，文风郁乎日以盛，白屋之贫，则今犹昔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312899_comment'></div>县去行都里以千计者四，负笈一诣，费比中州数倍，州劝驾馈钱缗百，此天下都国所无，窭儒道敝，犹有失其常产者，南冠仕进不如北方之多，非艺之不敌，特病于地远而发身之难耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312899_comment'></div>淳祐元年，圣天子颁兴贤诏，凤㟵经义词赋皆预选，久郁忽伸，明府何君喜邑人之所喜，礼遇视故例有加，以风动百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312899_comment'></div>一日，升堂语诸生曰：「愚不敏，学制相乡，与衿佩日周旋，士习淳古，薰然有清献遗风，可敬也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312899_comment'></div>汉制，习先圣之术与计偕，县实给食，将久远利之，亟三百千之损，而更掌以学职，听民持所有抵而出之，复入则收其赢什二，积三岁，为羡钱若干，新贡士人五十千，合所得于州者，可不损家藏铢粒，但囊书襆被，足以优游往返先荐送。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312899_comment'></div>今还试者抑于贡额之狭，而激昂璧水，试者皆厚给有差，策名飞捷至，又助之犒，区条画目，纤悉曲尽，士驩然相告曰：「业患不精，何患裹粮之不充」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312899_comment'></div>自此西笑，惟一意温故知新，无复向来皇皇焉办装之窘，将又有清名高节如前修者出，惠岂细哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312899_comment'></div>凡力振人之匮缺，必艰难险阻备尝之人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312899_comment'></div>君虽身诗书之泽，未尝口齑盐之味，而拳拳为寒酸地，若深计其子孙于无穷，是真知斯文之为重，发于良心善性，油然不可御，天资过人远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312899_comment'></div>傥益之问学，充拓其功，用将大可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312899_comment'></div>琴堂主人奋繇布衣，扉屦相望，贡士库乃自君创始，他治状未暇论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312899_comment'></div>只此一事，已无忝特笔矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312899_comment'></div>余又怪近世士大夫欲盖其厉民之迹，必厚于内交士，谓游谈聚议，足以好丑我，浓墨大字，足以轻重我也，则礼貌焉，赠遗焉，惟恐少失欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312899_comment'></div>盖蠢且弱之，莫予毒也，则渔猎椎剥，苟可以自丰殖，无所不至，不知一得罪于百姓，已得罪于名教，虽日畀之千金，安能遏乡校议政者之喙！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312899_comment'></div>彼是非之心转移于小濡沫，是贱丈夫箪食豆羹见于色者，乌得为士乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312899_comment'></div>增城斗绝一隅，学者尽在庠序，乡居惟石滩为士区，至于深山穷谷，家牛犊，人耒耜，寥寥弦诵，声利于士信美矣，必充周于民而后其泽溥，君盍推所以膏润后进者施之田里，毋苛取，毋曲决，孰为之利必兴，孰为之害必除，则四民均受抚字，赐虽古鲁卓何以加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312899_comment'></div>君名籍，月湖尚书其祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312899_comment'></div>月湖在石城，送人赴省，有「道在功名小」之句，此意又超然利禄之表，试与友朋味之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312899_comment'></div>五年上巳日，郡人李昴英记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1312899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年4月</a>　在广州。有词。作品：念奴娇（麦秋时候）<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　在广州。有文。作品：学士林君墓志铭。林隐君墓志铭。<div id='poem_1312911' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312911' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312911?labeling=true' target='_blank'>学士林君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312911")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312911_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312911'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312911'>君讳植，字建之，谱系古汴名阅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312911_comment'></div>国朝南渡初，乃先世著作郎佐郎俛始徙其族浮光，绝复规菟裘，遂定居于闽之长溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312911_comment'></div>厥后簪缨代不乏人，如家汴时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312911_comment'></div>迨君之曾大父坦，随季父宦游南海，遂之番禺家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312911_comment'></div>坦生君之王父清臣，清臣生君之皇考申，早声场屋，为庠序冠冕，俪于扶风氏，生君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312911_comment'></div>甫髫龄，夐颖悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312911_comment'></div>暨长，娱色养，必愉必婉，以至于失怙恃，哀瘠终丧无嘉容，且终其身，濡露履霜之思弗少替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312911_comment'></div>噫，孝已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312911_comment'></div>夫孝为百行原，宜乎君之行著于乡，咸曰义人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312911_comment'></div>同胞五人，有鹡原急难，君屡蹈死弗顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312911_comment'></div>亲党里闬有窭不自赈者，有及期不能婚嫁者，君罄所蓄赈之，兹皆厚于事亲，故推其馀以往，所薄者厚也亦宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312911_comment'></div>使假君以年，则强为善当益充，惜也其数七七而止，宝祐甲寅正月初五日殁于正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312911_comment'></div>易箦之际，作数诗偈，皆蜕生死语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312911_comment'></div>悲夫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312911_comment'></div>君室陇西氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312911_comment'></div>子元申，弱冠嗜绩文，婚于玉牒时漘之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312911_comment'></div>女二人，长适予之长孙亨宝，次将笄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312911_comment'></div>戊午七月辛酉，龟筮袭吉，其孤泣血托槥竁于郡之永泰里虎栏之原，祔先茔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312911_comment'></div>余识其邱陇，铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1312911'>君义人，孝天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312911_comment'></div>世茂阀，喜余庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312911_comment'></div>宅大宵，閟魂永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312911_comment'></div>槚拱兮，后昆盛。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1312911_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312910' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312910?labeling=true' target='_blank'>林隐君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1257年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312910")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312910_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312910'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312910'>昔之以卓行名，不必皆仕者也，懿于一念，奇于一节，太史氏笔之则闻，灭没无传亦多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312910_comment'></div>南海林君，乡曲称好人焉，闿其名，端甫其字，讷然言，颓然貌，而所存踰人远甚，不心乎利名，不色乎喜怒，不耳乎人之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312910_comment'></div>屋阛阓中，恶其嚣，辟隙地于后，窠花盆荷，观鱼狎鹤，寄意尘表，或穷年不出户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312910_comment'></div>妖卒噪城下，官委之登陴执戈，为里闾先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312910_comment'></div>时窭民窘食，指囷以给，有述前古吉凶人，明验可为世劝戒者，君模本散布，费不赀不靳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312910_comment'></div>己乐善，且欲夫人皆为善；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312910_comment'></div>己不敢为恶，且欲夫人皆不为恶，用心类如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312910_comment'></div>安然一生，七十有一岁而终，将以宝祐七年八月甲申窆之于番禺县峨官山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312910_comment'></div>子一人名洪，娶余女弟者，拜且泣，以铭请，可书于其人，不于其姻，曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1312910'>秉彝之真，古之遗民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312910_comment'></div>茂其后昆，此为种德之根。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312910_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　在广州。有诗。作品：送舶使周申。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年</a>　在广州。施财所建海珠寺成，僧鉴义作《海珠山慈度寺记》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1257&endYear=1257')">1257年8月9日</a>　在广州。卒，谥忠简，赐葬增城县丰湖山。<br /></div>
-----end

清远

-----title
杭州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6c45966ec7414f15932a9ef982c17bfc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6c45966ec7414f15932a9ef982c17bfc");'><span id='6c45966ec7414f15932a9ef982c17bfc_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>，23岁</div><div id='6c45966ec7414f15932a9ef982c17bfc' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1223&endYear=1223')">1223年</a>　在临安。第一次参加科举未中。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='defff5bd9556490d8732b917392cc79b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("defff5bd9556490d8732b917392cc79b");'><span id='defff5bd9556490d8732b917392cc79b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>，26岁</div><div id='defff5bd9556490d8732b917392cc79b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　在临安。春，登王会龙榜鼎甲第三名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年3月</a>　在临安。有捷书寄回。作品：丙戌科过省第一捷书。第二家书。第三书。<div id='poem_1312831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌科过省第一捷书<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312831")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312831_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1312831_0'>① 三月十八日捷子到广州，二十日到石滩。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312831'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312831'>某顿首百拜上覆大人朝议、亚妈孺人：某兹者荷先祖馀庆，大人阴骘，省试叨冒第三名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312831_comment'></div>自顾识浅才疏，何足当此，今因捷走报，谨写数字，以实其信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312831_comment'></div>然乡间前此无报三名前之例，必有无厌之求，亦宜权其轻重，多不过为政首可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312831_comment'></div>恐州县有礼议，大人可谋之亲知谙识者，随时区处，即此报知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312831_comment'></div>他冀精卫寝食，以迓鸿祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312831_comment'></div>某此来合受推官文林郎出身，乃庙堂送阙，亦候在外，待榜者毕至，方始唱名赐袍笏，圣上御便殿以颁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312831_comment'></div>仍旧例入局，待注受毕日，七月初必有归期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312831_comment'></div>谨此拜覆，伏乞尊览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312831_comment'></div>某百拜上覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312831_comment'></div>某烦一哥覆知大人，门径只宜依旧，不必加粉饰，遇某旧亦烦一哥呼名致谢。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312831_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312832' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312832' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312832?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌科过省第二家书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312832")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312832_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312832'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312832'>某顿首百拜上覆大人朝议、妈妈恭人：即辰季春，恭惟尊候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312832_comment'></div>某兹者叨冒正奏第三，无非大人平日积德之验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312832_comment'></div>但开榜之后，百费丛集，租一屋在学前，庶得王魁、张魁亦在左侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312832_comment'></div>某所赁之屋，一月二十券，捷人与诸人来贺亦五十券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312832_comment'></div>受劄之始，凡百物件，皆是新置，如买轿皂衫袍、带幞头、朝靴、一身衣服，轿番四名，每月二十馀千，书司厅子二名，每月亦十五千，已至借仆一日十馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312832_comment'></div>况某不谙此间新第事体，只得挈张上舍德明事与之商榷，庶得适宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312832_comment'></div>日间供膳，皆是己出，出二元信费二十千，未用一百馀券。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312832_comment'></div>自惟窘乏不能措，只得转假之乡人，候回日偿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312832_comment'></div>有便可报陈宅，必有钱助费，但非亲实人，不容付之来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312832_comment'></div>书铺来呈丙辰科事例，到五月中方唱名入局，以至受阙，并其他礼仪亦七月初方毕，到冬方有拜侍之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312832_comment'></div>所喜二状元相处甚得，有事必日来相报，出入皆同行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312832_comment'></div>大魁台州人，三十四岁，榜眼亦台州人，六十馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312832_comment'></div>凡见主司及朝士，皆与之同，及见邹尚书，彼再三丁宁，未要相见诸朝士，某自此不出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312832_comment'></div>诸同年及乡曲相识官员，日间相见常一二十人，只得奔走报谒，不容已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312832_comment'></div>某兹者本经出王太傅定房、参详丁郎中黼、知举邹尚书应龙，论在林太博良显，策未知在谁房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312832_comment'></div>三场未经改削，未敢附去，恐有人问，但以试官所批示之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312832_comment'></div>某此回例受推官，已令人寻访江西、广西诸处，自揣疏于吏事，亦须一年以上可也，亦但言其概。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312832_comment'></div>已至两处店主人书铺，亦须百以上千，请两人作四六，亦须百千，事体大概始末非千券不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312832_comment'></div>乡间风俗薄恶，多言某受人系着不可信，某新得一第，尚要前程久远。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1312832_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312833' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312833' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312833?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌科过省第三家书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312833")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312833_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312833'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312833'>某伏以春律向盈，韶光未减，恭惟大人朝奉、亚妈孺人尊候动止万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312833_comment'></div>某自得捷，当夜即发家书与捷子，又附一运司，走文字人想皆到矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312833_comment'></div>然潮州陈子谅必争先，但以家书为实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312833_comment'></div>犒捷之资，必候潮、广两处人俱齐，方始酌其轻重，不可作两项支与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312833_comment'></div>某尝会张魁，渠云乡曲捷人必待八九月自归，方始结付，乃其乡例也，恐未有钱，推以待某归尤佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312833_comment'></div>小人无厌，骤多与之，彼必求索无已，更在斟酌轻重，合数报人，共二百上下可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312833_comment'></div>某自归榜后，终日奔走，及归安下处，则诸公来访，及同年诸友相见，求入局者甚众，应酬无暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312833_comment'></div>来见邹先生，丁宁勿出，某恪守此戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312833_comment'></div>然程中书、陈中书皆遣人来请见，不容不往，以至某文字出渠房者皆往一见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312833_comment'></div>然诸公以某远方人，忽在前列，皆有愿见之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312833_comment'></div>凡所造见，甚荷温接，相见必问堂上，及闻某具庆，则歆羡不已，又问大人之年，某乙未对，尤加羡焉，其问娶否，则以已缀亲对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312833_comment'></div>书铺呈甲辰例，唱名在五月十二，缘其年混补，别来试所未闲，今岁既无混补，必须待出局及注差了毕，必七月终方有归期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312833_comment'></div>前日局中合干人来参，书吏、厅子、虞候、上名事官，每位三四十，某不敢留，使且待入局。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312833_comment'></div>京城桂玉之地，日费不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312833_comment'></div>王魁缀其同舍宁国府杜丈之女，岳翁为之支遣，张魁乃宰执侍从，撰述文字人，故诸公送馈良厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312833_comment'></div>惟某乏素，其接待礼数、出入仪从只得勉强随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312833_comment'></div>乡间义约钱一百券，带来四小铤，梁干又借去一笏，虽鬻之笏，犹有窘乏之忧，不免就施丈假借，渠又要归还七百足，更与渠商榷如何，势亦只得就渠借也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312833_comment'></div>家亦不必附钱与之，但龙涎香可买数两，素馨汤、茶饼之类，可买二三十瓶作人事，戚家苏合香丸、感应丸亦买数两来，更白拂手数条云云。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1312833_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　在临安。致书崔与之以表培育之恩。四月，崔与之有《菊坡回札》作品：致菊坡书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　在临安。有捷书寄回。作品：第四书。第五书。<div id='poem_1312834' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312834' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312834?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌科过省第四家书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312834")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312834_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312834'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312834'>某百拜上覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312834_comment'></div>即辰清和在候，恭惟大人朝奉、亚妈宜人尊候起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312834_comment'></div>某伏自尘忝之后，三附问安之书，想已俱到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312834_comment'></div>后遇乡间补试诸丈，询及家间动静，三月廿八日某人抵京，复接家书，深用慰浣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312834_comment'></div>某自箭桥移居学前，非报谒官员不敢轻出，凡事不敢轻举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312834_comment'></div>张德明以私试回斋，适惠州朱新恩篆至，某遂校之同楼，复留一房以待伦耀卿，而四月初彼犹未至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312834_comment'></div>日来诸厅贺吏已拨剔稍定，惟是同年之求入局者，多挟朝贵，或托相知，颇为所挠，只得随轻重区处，至于潮、惠、南雄诸同年，既是一路，不容不存之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312834_comment'></div>唱名亦未有日子，想只在五月初间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312834_comment'></div>所费浩繁，已就施丈借五百券，家间亦不必寄钱来用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312834_comment'></div>若有所争不多，不必与较，若大段相远，某做一道理，此不足虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312834_comment'></div>某前者已修劄达之陈宅，不知彼曾来相贺否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312834_comment'></div>朱新恩篆文雅且贤，与之相处甚得，彼遂有续弦之意，大人便问发与令往说之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312834_comment'></div>朱丈乙巳生，可与为亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312834_comment'></div>邱丈亦知其五行，若消耗之，便中垂示。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312834_comment'></div>有一劄达之广平公，少叙谢意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312834_comment'></div>人旋甚亟，漕台仓舶书未发，尚需别进，未由省侍，伏乞倍加调护，以介鼎来之祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312834_comment'></div>某下情祈祝之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312834_comment'></div>某百拜上覆大人朝奉、亚妈宜人、六叔朝奉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1312834_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙戌科过省第五家书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1226年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312835")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312835'>某顿首百拜上覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312835_comment'></div>即辰炎伏在候，暑气方殷，恭惟大人朝请、亚妈安人尊候起居万福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312835_comment'></div>某偕璧英在此如常，毋在留意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312835_comment'></div>念六月初二日陈全付至家书与陈宅书信皆到，官券五百贯已如数得讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312835_comment'></div>十三日上御文德殿，移御榻，临轩引见前三甲人三名，前作一班，相去才咫尺，日表龙姿，俨然在前，馀四甲、五甲人只在殿门之外，不及见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312835_comment'></div>礼毕，三名前就幕次，各赐食七品，罗满几案，精美可挹，累科所无也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312835_comment'></div>中贵、快行、卫士来索谢恩诗，即时就换袍笏，是时驾已入内，但抱敕黄拜殿门而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312835_comment'></div>三名先谢而出，即重戴乘马，所喝迎导如每科仪，但未过太庙，不审其仪也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1226&endYear=1226')">1226年</a>　在临安。长子将仕郎、转泽议郎寿道公生。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='4fe38a27714f43ad9664c21162317ecf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4fe38a27714f43ad9664c21162317ecf");'><span id='4fe38a27714f43ad9664c21162317ecf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1239')">1236-1239年</a>，36-39岁</div><div id='4fe38a27714f43ad9664c21162317ecf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年</a>　在临安。陛见，上奏。作品：端平丙申召除太博赐金奏札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年10月</a>　在临安。以太学博士召试馆职。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年11月</a>　在临安。除校书郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1236&endYear=1236')">1236年12月</a>　在临安。兼荣王府教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年1月</a>　在临安。改兼沂靖惠王府教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　在临安。三至七月间，转朝散郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年7月</a>　在临安。为宗正丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　在临安。秋，主持科举考试，被誉“得人”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1237&endYear=1237')">1237年</a>　在临安。有诗一首。作品：送族子春叟游西广。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年6月22日</a>　在临安。有文一篇。作品：书亡友张德明拥书楼。<div id='poem_1312881' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312881' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312881?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书士友张德明拥书楼</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年6月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312881")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312881_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312881'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312881'>余友张君，讳允迪，字德明，奇伟士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312881_comment'></div>自言出曲江文献公派，尝都城共邸，见其挟册竟画夜吟不辍，心甚敬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312881_comment'></div>无何，挈入璧流斋房就访焉，则壁横墨本二大字曰「拥书」，盖菊坡笔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312881_comment'></div>谓余曰：「某不才，辱乡达尊不鄙夷，其敢暴弃而战」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312881_comment'></div>其艺南宫辄北俛，就西廊试入前龟，迄不肉食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312881_comment'></div>余来宝安登其藏书楼，二大字宛其旧识，而故人隔世久矣，为之怆然，且仰叹大老先生乐与后进，惜天不寿斯人，少副所期也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312881_comment'></div>其三子斗文、翼文、光济，皆力学，克支门户，皆与漕计，自此能刻厉以成先志，则德明犹不死也，勉旃！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312881_comment'></div>嘉熙二年六月二十二日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312881_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年</a>　在临安。有诗一首。作品：送魁星与李子先。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年10月</a>　在临安。以直秘阁新知赣州，不拜。奉诏召崔与之还朝，有奏，除著作郎。迁大宗丞。作品：嘉熙戊戌奏札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1238&endYear=1238')">1238年12月</a>　在临安。有文。作品：书赵经干彦捍自鸣録。跋陈光庭所藏蒋实斋遗墨。<div id='poem_1312894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书赵经干彦捍自鸣录</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312894")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312894'>赵君御贼龙川，余方阖户恤居不得耳，颠末逆卒犯城以后事，则身其间，历历犹在眼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312894_comment'></div>是时肉食者争藏深遁远，寇退，亟呈身从而论功者亦众矣，君入与毗富道兵偕，自言溯韶溪趣之来援，似权以济事，而心未暴白于人，竟为法受恶，朝廷徐知其无他过，赐之环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312894_comment'></div>访余，出一编曰：「将持此鸣其不平，请为我一语，以證余生平不解绝物，而笔不逐世情」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312894_comment'></div>君异时督捕，诚有跋履之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312894_comment'></div>今自惠来，此邦人士相唁问不绝于馆，亦必有人心未能忘者，是则可录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312894_comment'></div>嘉熙戊戌腊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312894_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋陈光庭所藏蒋实斋遗墨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1238年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312875")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312875'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312875'>细数在世繇科级梯贵显凡几，能全节始终有几，容容温饱，固不足算，乖初心而谬末路，良可悯惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312875_comment'></div>方老奸擅权，以区区官爵笼天下士，鄙夫争吞炭为哑，以媒进取，一世习熟，谓敢言为狂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312875_comment'></div>实斋蒋公始召，忽大声长鸣于仗马间，聩者愕，默者愧，正论命脉，赖以挽回，其忧时爱主之忠，甚至于病且死不渝也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312875_comment'></div>科目得如此，士庶亦不忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312875_comment'></div>陈君元实布衣时登其门最久，而密贮遗墨盈幅，读之凛凛犹有生气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312875_comment'></div>元实今尉增江，甚公，甚廉，甚恕，使家稍抑之，群邑人叩台府乞留，非术驱利诱使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312875_comment'></div>观其字与公之名斋同，益信端人端友，平日相资讲切，皆实理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312875_comment'></div>百里人心德之，不忘其实学，功用小验云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312875_comment'></div>嘉熙戊戌腊。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年5月</a>　在临安。兼史馆校勘。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年5月</a>　在临安。兼权兵部郎官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='029f5e1e172d49f38b6f2f81f9d1b512_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("029f5e1e172d49f38b6f2f81f9d1b512");'><span id='029f5e1e172d49f38b6f2f81f9d1b512_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>，39岁</div><div id='029f5e1e172d49f38b6f2f81f9d1b512' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　在临安。以亲老丐外便养。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年9月</a>　在临安。除直秘阁、福建建宁宪仓提举。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年9月</a>　在临安。方大琮有《送俊明李提举（三首）》赠别。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='66d7d1e2e23f4e36a102a55a9cf69f1e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("66d7d1e2e23f4e36a102a55a9cf69f1e");'><span id='66d7d1e2e23f4e36a102a55a9cf69f1e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1247')">1246-1247年</a>，46-47岁</div><div id='66d7d1e2e23f4e36a102a55a9cf69f1e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年3月16日</a>　在临安。有文。作品：题菊坡水调歌头后。<div id='poem_1312862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题菊坡水调歌头后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312862")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312862'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312862'>清献崔公《剑阁》赋长短句，卷卷爱君忧国，遑恤身计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312862_comment'></div>此意类《出师表》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312862_comment'></div>雅趣欲结茅庾岭边，一琴一鹤，繇湘桂归南海，竟不得践绿阴青子约，然幅巾藜杖，徜徉老圃寒花间十有六年，晏岁之乐，不减洛中耆英也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312862_comment'></div>好事者揭此词山中，惜非公手迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312862_comment'></div>某敬以所藏本授横浦校官赖君栋，使刻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312862_comment'></div>文献张公始凿岭路而未有祠，着公同龛为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312862_comment'></div>此则地主事，非过客所得专也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312862_comment'></div>淳祐六年三月既望，门人李昴英。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312862_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。任侍右郎官，上奏劾三奸邪，不报。作品：淳祐丙午侍右郎官赴阙奏札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。再上奏，求选拔人才，荐方大琮。帝书姓名于御屏。作品：第二札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。乞申杜范、刘汉弼、徐元杰三贤之冤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。除右正言兼侍讲。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。刘克庄有《李昴英右正言制》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年10月1日</a>　在临安。有文。作品：淳祐丙午十月朔奏札。除正言上殿奏疏。<div id='poem_1312802' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312802' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312802?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除正言上殿奏疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312802")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312802_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312802'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312802'>臣生远迹孤，学肤识狭，陛下拔之疏散，俾缀谏曹，圣恩如天，誓图报塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312802_comment'></div>臣拜观国史，范镇擢知谏院，即上疏曰：「陛下置谏官者，所以为宗庙社稷计也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312802_comment'></div>为谏官而不以宗庙社稷事陛下，是不知谏官之任也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312802_comment'></div>拳拳之忠，首以正国本为言，臣何人斯，讵敢望镇万一，于忠国爱君之职分，则不敢不尽焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312802_comment'></div>臣闻正天下之大本贵乎豫，定天下之大计贵乎果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312802_comment'></div>三王家天下，其初心岂专为子孙地？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312802_comment'></div>所以弭争端于未萌，杜厉阶于未形，而欲措斯世于久安耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312802_comment'></div>副贰早建，所以系海内之望，成谋坚凝，所以释人心之疑，讵容一日稍缓哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312802_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下诞膺宝历，光绍鸿图，惟天惟祖宗岂私于陛下，将以垂统无穷，为万世开太平者望陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312802_comment'></div>春秋寖盛，苍震尚虚，群臣恳切交疏而力陈，四方倾耳翘首而耸听，几年于此矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312802_comment'></div>陛下环视而未有定向，迟回而不轻一发，事大体重，于谋始宜谨，非常情所能测识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312802_comment'></div>迩者谒飨宗庙，驳雾划开，惟天之眷，惟祖宗之灵，默赞大计，随洒宸章，选纳犹子，嘉名宠锡，圣意丕昭，朝野鼓舞，神祇欢悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312802_comment'></div>然虽有举棋将定之喜，不能无羽翼未成之虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312802_comment'></div>臣于此时，叨被亲擢，事莫此为大，谨以三说上渎圣聪，惟陛下垂听焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312802_comment'></div>一曰正名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312802_comment'></div>文帝即位初年，有司遽以建太子为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312802_comment'></div>今不可谓早计矣，历观往昔，当璧而拜之观，惟神之所予，有心无聊之欢，惟人之所付，是皆牵缠己私，不克断制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312802_comment'></div>陛下此一盛举，蔽自圣衷，度越前古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312802_comment'></div>出于同气，天属为最亲，储以继体，人道为极顺，倘或犹豫，能不动摇？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312802_comment'></div>名号未正，恐无以塞从旁之觊觎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312802_comment'></div>体统未一，恐无以收众望之归向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312802_comment'></div>谓宜亟正青盖车之制，伫开日重光之祥，侍膳问安，自此全天性之乐，主器承祧，足以衍国祚之长，天下咸曰吾君有子矣，则宗庙社稷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312802_comment'></div>普安郡王之封，宰臣请以冠属籍，高宗皇帝曰「可便为皇子」，此陛下所当法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312802_comment'></div>二曰保养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312802_comment'></div>保其身体，列职周官，养于掖庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312802_comment'></div>有汉故事，挺生岐嶷之质，犹在髫稚之年，必先葆固其天和，庶可自贻于哲命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312802_comment'></div>昔人有嗜鲍之动，戒有玉契之严，惟所关所系者不细，故防微杜渐者至悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312802_comment'></div>出入起居，宁卫防之过密，饥饱寒暑，必调适之得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312802_comment'></div>此天下之大器也，岂止于椟拱璧、培桐梓之譬哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312802_comment'></div>谓宜专属禁闼之尊，曲加抚摩之爱，宫人之老成谨厚者左右弥缝之，奇邪侧媚之人不得与乎其间，则宗庙社稷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312802_comment'></div>高宗皇帝因大臣宫人可托否之问，有曰「若不先择宫嫔，可虑之事更多」，陛下所当法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1312802_comment'></div>三曰教道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1312802_comment'></div>道之礼义，周过其历，傅之刑名，秦祚遽危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1312802_comment'></div>盖少成若天性，习惯如自然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1312802_comment'></div>古者有褓教，有齿学，莫不于其初而渐渍入之，是必妙选于师儒，所当涵养其德性，毋徒事章句之末技，毋但拘讲诵之常程，俾善言正行，日接于见闻，非心邪念，不萌于方寸，则凡朝夕宴处之际，无非薰陶淑迪之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1312802_comment'></div>又当择臣之有物望者，时视其德业之进，因以为内学之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1312802_comment'></div>他日恭敬温文发达于性资，孝友仁爱著闻于中外，则宗庙社稷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1312802_comment'></div>陈俊卿每入，必传经启沃，且殚讽谏之益，陛下必得若人而委之辅导可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1312802_comment'></div>厥今时艰未靖，国势未强，阴邪诪张于肘腋之间，敌气滋煽于边庭之外，消弭奸党，镇压群疑，全在此着。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1312802_comment'></div>臣愿陛下上念祖宗付托之不轻，下慰生灵徯望之甚切，决意建置，无堕因循，亿万载无疆之休，实根本乎此，惟陛下留神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1312802_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1312802_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年</a>　在临安。连上疏论史嵩之。作品：论史丞相疏。贴黄论史丞相。列奏史丞相疏。<div id='poem_1312803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论史丞相疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312803")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312803'>臣末学陋闻，误蒙睿知，擢联翠幄，获执麟经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312803_comment'></div>日昨进讲至鲁隐公二年郑人伐卫，因考寤生之无主，其恶根于城颖之寘母，以为世之大不忠，皆大不孝者为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312803_comment'></div>夫子无其位，故诛奸臣于直笔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312803_comment'></div>陛下操必罚之柄，昭惩恶之公，傥不孝于亲，且将不利于国者幸免焉，此岂圣人作经，有望于后之明天子之意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312803_comment'></div>臣曩在岭海间，竦聆陛下雷发英断，山拔巨奸，至于穷陬僻区之人，莫不欢呼鼓舞，日以俟谓之渡崖，确之徙新也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312803_comment'></div>踰年而秪闻二三邪党之贬，羽翼虽剪，元恶未除，天下已共疑而切议矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312803_comment'></div>臣今夏造朝，首乞明正渠魁之罪，圣意尚需迟而欠决，容德天涵，或以其未终丧，姑有待焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312803_comment'></div>今服阕近在于旬日，而官刑未举于司败，人言籍籍，通国皇惑，臣而隐嘿，言责谓何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312803_comment'></div>臣窃观昔之所谓四凶者，非如后世大奸剧恶之甚也，投畀魑魅，舜岂少恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312803_comment'></div>盖小人衷险裒狡，乘间辄发，一旦得志，则君子必被其祸，生民必罹其毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312803_comment'></div>有不胜穷者操之已蹙，盛古且然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312803_comment'></div>嵩之谲诈贪婪，狠愎残忍，罪浮于四凶，前后白简之所擢数，皂囊之所鸣攻，既详且悉，臣不敢更渎天听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312803_comment'></div>大抵其挟敌要君如秦桧，其嫉贤妒能如李林甫，其阴害忤己者如卢杞，其藉权宠、厚赀积如郑注，其与近习盘结如元载，其秽行丑声如杨国忠，其匿丧不持服如李定，其怀宰相不足为之心如宗楚客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312803_comment'></div>人臣有一于此，皆宜在诛绝之科，况身兼众恶乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312803_comment'></div>去位家居，日常齧齿握拳，书空击地，愤愤然规复出，以快报复，私布驶传于道路，多设狡窟于京都，赂贵近以觇伺人主之言动，结浮士以刺探中朝之议论，群不逞为之耳目，为之爪距者，在在布满也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312803_comment'></div>鸱枭乘暗，鼷鼯睨昏，磨虎狼之牙，喷蛇蜮之沫，意欲何为哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312803_comment'></div>鄙夫患失，无所不至，万一通神计行，回天力到，必将惩前日之轻失，积邪心而动，于恶无所不为矣，此天下之巨蠹，潜伏而未发，而曰此不复然灰耳，可惧哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312803_comment'></div>又况国本渐定，正要保持坚决，为宗社计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312803_comment'></div>人望稍聚，正要协比联固，为世道计；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312803_comment'></div>岁事少稔，正要涵润苏息，为生民计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312803_comment'></div>小人之根未去，宗社之危安，世道之升降，生民之休戚关焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1312803_comment'></div>利害晓然而未即加罚，或谓陛下外示宽洪之恩意，中寓羁縻之微权，卒有缓急，或堪倚仗，又臣之所未谕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1312803_comment'></div>盖自陛下收揽大柄，亲决万机以来，区画边防，亦未尝失事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1312803_comment'></div>人才，陛下之人才，兵财，陛下之兵财，自有而用之，若大臣降心相从，商量恰好，天下事岂难办集？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1312803_comment'></div>彼小人者于谋身则周密，于谋国则架漏，已试明验，大略可睹矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1312803_comment'></div>臣侧闻陛下有对越高庙神灵之诗，有「奸邪终摈斥」之句，则知定见不惑，定力不移，决不至来外邪以坏局面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1312803_comment'></div>然化弦更张，亦既久矣，而大纲领犹未正，大机括犹未定，此一事颠末未备，恐无以垂汗青、诏后世，陛下亦尝思及此乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1312803_comment'></div>章惇才免父丧，便提举洞霄宫，俄而得政，遂啸凶俦，毒善类，为国厉阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1312803_comment'></div>往辙可鉴，臣愚欲望陛下俯从舆议，独运精刚，亟烦宸札，寝嵩之服阕与宫观之命，仍削官爵，远窜荒裔，使群阴扫迹，众正伸气，于以安人心，于以寿国脉，天下幸甚！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1312803_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1312803_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1312803'>〔贴黄〕臣昨论奏史嵩之奸恶罪状，皆国人之公言，今既累日未蒙付出，欲乞陛下决行宗社大计，早赐区处，恭俟睿断。</div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1312803_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1312804' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312804' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312804?labeling=true' target='_blank'>列奏史丞相疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312804")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312804_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312804'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312804'>臣等各有疏论列史嵩之罪恶，俯伏俟命，未蒙报可，遂具劄白之二三大臣，冀其密勿开陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312804_comment'></div>近闻陛下宣引宰执，必有商搉，在朝莫不欢跃耸听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312804_comment'></div>窜责共驩之命又累日矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312804_comment'></div>嵩之得罪宗社，得罪纲常，通国一辞，谓宜诛绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312804_comment'></div>而陛下迟回至今，罪名未正，当明主可为忠言之时，而感动之难如此，岂非臣等敷词未能真切，不足以开悟渊听耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312804_comment'></div>岂非二三大臣无非畏避，不肯尽情以告陛下耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312804_comment'></div>又岂非诸大臣国人皆曰之公论，不足以胜阿谀之口耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312804_comment'></div>臣等窃谓臣之事君，犹子之事父，谏而不止，又敬不违，乃职分当然，谨不避鈇锧，联合以请，欲望陛下察臣等拳拳愚衷出于为国，早赐处分，以前所奏付外施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312804_comment'></div>傥臣等屡言不行，而强颜宪地，岂不上负陛下之亲擢，下负海内之责望乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312804_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312804_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。上疏请正嵩之罪。十二月，诏史嵩之致仕。作品：再论史丞相疏。<div id='poem_1312805' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312805' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312805?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论史丞相疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312805")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312805_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312805'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312805'>臣闻苏轼曰：「祖宗委任台谏，养其锐气，借之重权，所以折奸臣之萌也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312805_comment'></div>奸谋未成，犹当亟遏绝之，既滋蔓矣，除恶本或不力焉，岂祖宗设台谏初意哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312805_comment'></div>此臣所以早夜以思，忘寝与食也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312805_comment'></div>臣昨疏列史嵩之奸状，将涉兼旬，屡入催奏，未闻制可，圣意渊深，外庭未孚，始相顾而疑，今相语以忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312805_comment'></div>陛下一则曰保全大臣，二则曰保全大臣，恶盈其贯，显灼昭白，天地鬼神所不赦，陛下独委曲包容，惟恐伤之，圣度恢恢，前古未有，臣何敢不将顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312805_comment'></div>然事有害大祸深，与吾国势不并立者，则宁有犯无隐，求不负圣门之训，乃所以不负天子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312805_comment'></div>夫君视臣如手足，臣视君如腹心，相须之义然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312805_comment'></div>嵩之包藏祸心，窃据相位，不以事天事陛下，而视国家如仇，此凶人耳，罪人耳，复以大臣待之，可乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312805_comment'></div>自其漏我师期，于是乎有京洛之败，假挟北使，于是乎有邀索之辱，导敌入寇，于是乎有淮甸之祸，是为卖国之贼臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312805_comment'></div>席卷部内之帑藏，囊括诸路之利源，借国用匮乏之名，鹾贩货易，笼归私室，富且数倍于国，是为蠹国之盗臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312805_comment'></div>给谏宰掾，朋分杂布，以障蔽人主之耳目，以窃弄人主之威柄，是为擅国之强臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312805_comment'></div>科抑太繁而民怨，券给不均而兵怨，扼遏摧沮之过甚而士大夫怨，是为误国之奸臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312805_comment'></div>抽移江上之军，入补周庐之额，用意殊叵测，向非陛下洞烛邪奸，力拒不纳，且将为害国之乱臣矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312805_comment'></div>大臣以道事君者也，嵩之凶悖奸诈，阴险忮毒，于臣道何有！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312805_comment'></div>齐豹位司寇，作而不义，《春秋》书之曰盗，嵩之尚得为大臣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1312805_comment'></div>孟子曰：「无君无父，是禽兽也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1312805_comment'></div>以若所为，尚不得齿于人类，尚可以谓之大臣乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1312805_comment'></div>天下者祖宗之天下，所以植亿万年本根者深且固，而嵩之日寻斧斤焉，虽肆诸两观，未足以上慰祖宗在天之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1312805_comment'></div>踰两年而罪名未正，陛下宁不动心于见宗庙之时乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1312805_comment'></div>陛下刚健中正，与天同运，傥以姑息为至仁，以不断为盛德，是有春而无秋，有雨露而无霜雪雷霆，非天之所以为天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1312805_comment'></div>臣于嵩之无纤芥之怨，发于忠愤，不容但已，苟利社稷，一身之祸福所不暇计，欲望陛下尽取前后臣下所言书疏，参考其不道之本末，亟赐睿旨，并臣先所奏，付外施行，使天下臣民明知去邪之真意，千载而下竦服锄奸之伟断，臣退而渎犯天威之诛，死无所恨，区区血忱，惟陛下察之！</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1312805_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。上奏请肃朝仪而振朝纲。作品：论帝属贵臣不趋早朝奏札。<div id='poem_1312806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论帝属贵臣不趋早朝奏劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312806")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312806_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312806'>臣二十一日缀四参官起居，因俟候奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312806_comment'></div>窃观帝属之班，稀疏为甚，赤墀步武，殆类晨星，退而询问，则知迩者常参或秪一二人，趋趁夫鸣玉曳组，鹓列鹭行以进退，朝廷之礼貌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312806_comment'></div>冕旒端复，威颜咫尺，而着定在前，尚多旷阙，欲门庭之外，事事整肃，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312806_comment'></div>陛下大昕而南面，虽隆寒不惮，贵臣或连日不望清光，理恐未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312806_comment'></div>昔人有盛服假寐者，有驻车待漏者，夙兴匪懈，自是臣子分内事，况清晨一觐而退，他无职业，傥复于此忽略，岂一德尊天子之义乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312806_comment'></div>「辉辉睹明圣，济济行俊贤」，唐人形容早朝之盛若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312806_comment'></div>陛下正朝廷百官，要以心为本，欲其平旦清明，敬心油然而生，非但贵其仆仆拜起，以侈容貌采章之美也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312806_comment'></div>臣以为其间真有采薪之忧，不能造朝者，当察其情，至于无他故而屡不至焉，是则豢安成惰，可不略加警策乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312806_comment'></div>欲望陛下申儆有位，使咸造在朝，庶几人心不玩，主势益尊，所以肃朝仪而振朝纲，亦非小节也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。有奏论陈韡，不纳。作品：论陈枢密疏。<div id='poem_1312808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论陈枢密疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312808")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312808_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312808'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312808'>臣闻罪莫大于背国，恶莫大于庇奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312808_comment'></div>两地之重职，为大臣一言之发，关系不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312808_comment'></div>倘或立异论以沮大计，怀私意以昧公非，群情为之动摇，众口从而噂沓，良由心术颇僻，识见猥庸，用过其分，不觉呈露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312808_comment'></div>事既关于宗社，责难逭于简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312808_comment'></div>臣切见通议大夫、参知政事兼同知枢密院事陈韡自负胆略，亦锐功名，江闽讨寇，虽屡书劳，妄杀平民，颇多枉滥，后来调兵过江之轻举，遂至匹马只轮之不返，志广才疏，前功俱废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312808_comment'></div>且莫当于一面，尚可望其远猷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312808_comment'></div>陛下念其久闲，擢之近辅，勉思所以上答主恩，下副人望可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312808_comment'></div>理财专局，略无设施，褊性狠态，时复妄发，此犹未足深责也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312808_comment'></div>国本始定，神人所同喜，韡独出语不逊，识者骇愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312808_comment'></div>奸相负罪，神人所同怒，韡犹盛称其孝，识者忿之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1312808_comment'></div>陛下决天下之大计，去天下之巨蠹，断自圣心，超越前古，身为执政，不能从容密赞，乃持论悖谬如此，心事可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1312808_comment'></div>夫沮抑普安之事，非秦桧之奸不敢为，而营救蔡确者，虽以范纯仁、王存之贤不免黜罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1312808_comment'></div>臣采之公论，皆谓韡之叨尘已极，矧其猜忮嗜杀，使自得恣流毒，必广斥去为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1312808_comment'></div>臣旧尝为之属，不敢以私情废公法，欲望陛下察其非忠，退之以礼，职名藩寄，华其暮途，爰示宽恩之曲全，式彰清议之不贷，使臣子各厉忠纯之节，天下明知是非之公，实世道之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1312808_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1312808_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。有奏论赵与 ，不纳。作品：论赵京尹疏。<div id='poem_1312809' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312809' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312809?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论赵京尹疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312809")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312809_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312809'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312809'>臣闻国朝旧制，不以宗室居宰辅，以其有逼近之嫌也，其为虑远矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312809_comment'></div>畿府号众大之区，委寄隆重，有利权，有兵柄，有狡黠健悍之徒为之分布奔走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312809_comment'></div>是虽非宰辅之位，而权力过之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312809_comment'></div>纵使处是职者果宗贤，且难久任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312809_comment'></div>盖积威积惠之深，人心所重在彼，非国家之便也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312809_comment'></div>今有帅雄繁之地，涉嫌疑之迹，而顽然不知引退者，众情皇惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312809_comment'></div>人言权故事，优畀职名，遣镇外服，不惟国本安固，可以一人心之趋向，乃所以福与缙于安全之地，亦亲亲之仁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312809_comment'></div>小臣不识忌讳，罪当万死，惟陛下赦之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312809_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1312809_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。有奏。作品：缴奏札子。<div id='poem_1312810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴奏劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1246年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312810")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312810'>臣一介孤远，误蒙睿简，擢之谏职，非由大臣荐进，举朝共知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312810_comment'></div>臣朝夕自厉，惟知报君父，惟知卫社稷，惟知利国家，一身祸福，且不暇恤，虽圣谕亦不敢阿顺，讵肯俛受他人风旨哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312810_comment'></div>臣今早上殿读第一劄将毕，陛下问臣次劄所论何人，臣以陈韡、赵与缙对，天语再三止之，令不须展读，臣辩说移时，圣意坚执倍力，亦不许纳奏劄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312810_comment'></div>秪得跼蹐而退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312810_comment'></div>缘臣所言二臣皆于国本有关，既切宗社，皆是国人之公论，臣所职者言，若置之不闻，而捃摭琐碎，以塞谏纸，则物议交责，臣何颜立于风宪之地乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312810_comment'></div>谨不避诛殛，连元本缴进，欲望圣意察臣愚衷，秪是为国，非出于胸臆之私，特垂省览，亟赐付外施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312810_comment'></div>仍乞睿旨放臣归田里，实荷圣恩保全之赐！</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1312810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。有疏论柔佞亲忠直。作品：淳祐丙午十二月正言奏札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。有诗送别高斯得。作品：送高礼部不妄知严州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1246&endYear=1246')">1246年12月</a>　在临安。挂冠归，三学书生以诗饯公国门外。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1247&endYear=1247')">1247年</a>　暮春，归广州，父老争持彩帜郊迎焉。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2f205a2071c6498b81e65caf3d7f36d3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2f205a2071c6498b81e65caf3d7f36d3");'><span id='2f205a2071c6498b81e65caf3d7f36d3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1255')">1254-1255年</a>，54-55岁</div><div id='2f205a2071c6498b81e65caf3d7f36d3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年1月</a>　在临安。除大宗正卿，赴阙，兼国史院编修、宝録院检讨。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在临安。上奏劾贾似道、丁大全。作品：宝祐甲寅宗正卿上殿奏札。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年9月</a>　在临安。乞罢幸西太乙，帝皆纳。除兼侍讲。作品：乞罢幸西太乙札子。<div id='poem_1312812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢幸西太乙劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1254年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312812")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312812'>方四郊多垒，此正卧薪尝胆时，湖山在目，日涉游观，道路颇遥，驾还必暮，意料之外，事非一端。</div><div id='poem_sentence_0_1312812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年11月3日</a>　在临安。赞皇子忠王祺冠礼，进太常卿，礼成，除右史，迁左史，兼权吏部右侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1254&endYear=1254')">1254年</a>　在临安。除龙图阁待制、尚书吏部侍郎，加中大夫，开国男。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在临安。上疏劾卢允升、董宋臣，不报。作品：乞行御史洪天锡劾阉寺之言疏。<div id='poem_1312813' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312813' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312813?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞行御史洪天锡劾阉寺之言疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312813")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312813_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312813'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312813'>今岁以来，天变频仍，正当修人事以应之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312813_comment'></div>倘人事又变，是以变弭变，天怒何从而释耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312813_comment'></div>台臣非他官比，今以劾寺珰而去，纪纲紊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312813_comment'></div>是非易置，去留倒施，人事之变，孰大于此！</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1312813_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1255&endYear=1255')">1255年</a>　在临安。再疏乞与洪天锡俱贬，不报，与洪天锡俱辞官归。<div id='poem_1312814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再疏乞与洪天锡俱贬</a><span class='authorDate'>（1255年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312814")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312814'>迩来北司专恣，日甚一日，他人不敢言，察臣天锡独言之，俄而解言职以去，中外莫不骇愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312814_comment'></div>始天锡登朝，臣实荐之，如不行其言，乞俱贬。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1312814_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
长汀
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='98c1e18e9c8246bd9f2453d921e50e86_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("98c1e18e9c8246bd9f2453d921e50e86");'><span id='98c1e18e9c8246bd9f2453d921e50e86_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1232')">1229-1232年</a>，29-32岁</div><div id='98c1e18e9c8246bd9f2453d921e50e86' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年</a>　在汀州推官任。汀州守虐下，悍兵欲杀守，李昴英以身翼，守得免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年10月</a>　在汀州。有诗。作品：跋陈侯赠曹贡元士圭诗。跋第二首。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1229&endYear=1229')">1229年</a>　在汀州。次子守道生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1230&endYear=1230')">1230年</a>　在汀州，任推官。有文一篇。作品：送周士元序。<div id='poem_1312839' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312839' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312839?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送周士元序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1230年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312839")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312839_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312839'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312839'>贫无以养，由也伤之，菽水尽欢，子谓之孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312839_comment'></div>士之身于贫，甑釜尘，箪瓢空，安处而无求焉，固也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312839_comment'></div>若夫半菽不充，亲无欢颜，未免皇皇奔走以追斗升，岂获已哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312839_comment'></div>余馆清漳逆旅，邂逅宁德周士元，问其来，愀然曰：「双亲耄矣，瓶无储粟，不遥千里，将控诸谊人而未遭也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312839_comment'></div>乐岁闻之人仰事不足之叹，不觉涕下，执其手语之曰：「子处人所未尝之贫，而为人所不能之孝，因至贫而至孝著焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312839_comment'></div>使子有二顷田，侍两安舆，庖猩熊，裘狐貉，以顺适其志，则子之职尽，而孝之名何有是！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312839_comment'></div>如临难捐躯，而得忠义名，非幸也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312839_comment'></div>夫孝者诚之发，诚至则天通地感，况人乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1312839_comment'></div>世固有拥厚资家，垂白犹健，以备甘旨之奉者，见子之来，必忻然同志，举千金以赒子，身美官，戏䌽娱侍，以遂禄养之志者，见子之来，必欢然锡类，辍三釜之馀以赠子，子姑持此诚以往，必有诚于孝者，应如胶漆，如符契矣，子其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1312839_comment'></div>绍定庚寅月正李昴英序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1312839_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1231&endYear=1231')">1231年</a>　在汀州，任推官。三子志道生。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1232&endYear=1232')">1232年</a>　在汀州，任推官。朱积宝合磜寇围汀州，平之，除太学正。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
建宁
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9462c7bad127481280986dd675a51da2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9462c7bad127481280986dd675a51da2");'><span id='9462c7bad127481280986dd675a51da2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>，39岁</div><div id='9462c7bad127481280986dd675a51da2' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在建宁。是年，有奏札。作品：嘉熙己亥著作郎奏札。第二札。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在建宁。是年，有文。作品：跋清献崔公手墨。<div id='poem_1312861' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312861' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312861?labeling=true' target='_blank'>跋清献崔公手墨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312861")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312861_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312861'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312861'>嘉熙己亥，某在著庭，清献崔公自南海寄书来，别纸如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312861_comment'></div>公拜集贤相，天子遣中使踰岭趣行，且赐金二百两，治装蒲轮日在门，而公之病已深矣，累疏力辞，始得请以金付武臣邓祖禹护纳内库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312861_comment'></div>盖公帅乡部时，祖禹实为事务官，所以委之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312861_comment'></div>此役他人所难，而祖禹不惮劳费，似知慕独乐园之守园者，亦可尚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312861_comment'></div>偶阅公手泽，俾模刻而藏之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312861_comment'></div>淳祐五年元日。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1312861_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='712ac907f7eb4dc286c7f255d15f6538_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("712ac907f7eb4dc286c7f255d15f6538");'><span id='712ac907f7eb4dc286c7f255d15f6538_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1240')">1239-1240年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='712ac907f7eb4dc286c7f255d15f6538' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　在建宁。是年，有文。作品：书泷水赵宰汝軏生祠后。<div id='poem_1312880' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312880' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312880?labeling=true' target='_blank'>书泷水赵宰汝軏生祠后</a><span class='authorDate'>（1239年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312880")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312880_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312880'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312880'>端平二年二月七日，狂卒曾忠啸众突南海城，余缒出行其垒，且周晓以逆顺祸福，群凶帖听，遁而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312880_comment'></div>又四年，读泷水民立《赵令君生祠记》，而后知贼据古端日，康之人大恐，泷境内鮀黎獠假防县为名，鸣刃噪庭下，令从容折以理，即解散去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312880_comment'></div>时菊坡公帅乡部，如此好汉，惜郡将不以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312880_comment'></div>余方在幕府，实负蔽贤愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312880_comment'></div>赵君有靖百里功，未尝口，微邑人载之碣，殆不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312880_comment'></div>今士大夫几大树将军，矧宗室子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312880_comment'></div>君名汝軏，敏才而力学，所至有政可称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1312880_comment'></div>南海李昴英书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1312880_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年</a>　在建宁。吏治澄清。岁大荒，捐俸赈贷，活饥人甚衆。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1239&endYear=1239')">1239年11月</a>　在建宁。崔与之卒，请归服心丧，不许。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　在建宁。因彭方劾，李昴英罢，奉其父李天斐归。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年4月</a>　在建宁。有文。作品：题郑上舍玠大学䇿稿。<div id='poem_1312859' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1312859' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1312859?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郑上舍玠大学策稿</a><span class='authorDate'>（1240年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(27440, "南宋", "李昴英", "poem_title_1312859")'>李昴英</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1312859_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1312859'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1312859'>士试于有司曰时文，志于得而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1312859_comment'></div>郑君对策天子学，乃极言天下事，皆有关于君德，有裨于世道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1312859_comment'></div>方鲠论崛起，与国论争锋，祸且不避，宁得失计耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1312859_comment'></div>胸中所存，定非寻常诸生拔尺寸比，是真不负皇朝淑养之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1312859_comment'></div>衡文者拔其尤，则公论犹未泯，可为斯文贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1312859_comment'></div>君其坚此志勿渝，厚其养勿馁，大建立于世，垂声名无穷，毋使人曰此徒议论之士，吾党所望也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1312859_comment'></div>嘉熙庚子四月。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1312859_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年4月</a>　在建宁。有词。作品：兰陵王（燕穿幕）<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2b7f17698ffb4f0ea3a04822c6c7da01_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2b7f17698ffb4f0ea3a04822c6c7da01");'><span id='2b7f17698ffb4f0ea3a04822c6c7da01_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>，40岁</div><div id='2b7f17698ffb4f0ea3a04822c6c7da01' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1240&endYear=1240')">1240年</a>　在建宁。有诗。作品：寄赠竹隐李聘君。<br /></div>
-----end
